Japanese Troops Forcibly Occupy Beining Railway 69

▲ Section Chiefs and Station Masters Replaced by Employees of the South Manchuria Railway

▲ Through Traffic to Guan Nei Limited to Shanhaiguan

Tianjin Correspondence: Since the capture of Jinzhou, Japanese troops have continued to advance to Suizhong, seeking to connect with the Japanese troops stationed in Shanhaiguan. The Chinese troops at the forefront are the 9th Brigade under He Zhuguo, stationed in Guan Nei. A few days ago, Brigade Commander He, fearing further attacks by the Japanese troops, specifically discussed the matter with the Japanese commander stationed in Shanhaiguan and went to Suizhong together to declare to the Japanese troops that the Chinese troops had completely withdrawn to Guan Nei and that there was no need for further military action. He Zhuguo is a graduate of the Japanese Military Academy and is proficient in Japanese. After this negotiation, the situation seemed to ease slightly. In fact, since the Chinese troops had already withdrawn, the Japanese troops had no targets for hostility. However, the Beining Railway, from Beiping to Shenyang, a total length of over 843 kilometers, takes 21 and a half hours to reach its destination. Shanhaiguan is conveniently located at the midpoint of Beining. Since the September 18th Incident last year, although the section outside the pass has been able to reach Huanggu Tun, in fact, all freight and passenger traffic has decreased by eighty or ninety percent. According to the railway's statistics, the loss from transportation alone exceeds 5 million yuan in three months. Other losses, such as the damage from Japanese artillery fire and bombs, are not included. After Jinzhou was captured, through traffic on the section outside the pass was completely suspended again. During the height of the war, most of the employees at the stations felt their lives were in danger and returned to Tianjin. The railway bureau, considering that the railway was related to international transportation and had British investment, could not allow the Japanese troops to ravage it, so it sent Mr. Stealey (British), head of the Motive Power Department, and foreign employee Baker to the front to negotiate with the Japanese troops, intending to discuss ways to resume traffic and ordered the employees who had returned to Tianjin to return to their original posts outside the pass. The Japanese troops did not allow it. It is now heard that the Japanese side has taken over the trunk and branch lines of the Beining section outside the pass in the name of the puppet Northeast Transportation Committee and has renamed the section outside the pass the Shanfeng Railway. In addition to transferring Kan Duo, Director of the Siping-Taonan Railway Bureau, to serve as Director of the Shanfeng Bureau, the section chiefs and station masters of each section have also been appointed and replaced by employees of the South Manchuria Railway. The railway signs have also been changed. The special train sent by the railway bureau here to repair telegraphs and telephones only reached Suizhong yesterday (the 9th). Beyond this point, it was stopped by the Japanese troops and could not proceed. In addition, all the telephone and telegraph machines at the stations outside the pass were taken away by the Japanese troops after this major destruction by the Japanese troops. Each station along the route has twenty or thirty Japanese soldiers stationed. It is also heard that the Japanese troops have also sent engineering teams to repair the damaged sections along the way by a deadline, preparing to open traffic on the section from Shenyang to Shanhaiguan. The Japanese intention to destroy China's transportation industry and forcibly seize the rights of the Beining Railway is already very clear. (January 10th)

Abolition of the Guangzhou National Government 70

▲ Extraordinary Conference to End Before the 15th

▲ The Southwest Executive Department and Other Organizations Are Quite Simple

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since the unified government was established, the mission of the Guangzhou National Government has been completed and there is no need for it to exist. It was officially abolished on New Year's Day this year by sending a telegram. However, after the abolition, the resolutions of the Fourth Plenary Session of the Kuomintang in Guangzhou will still be followed. The Southwest Executive Department of the Central Executive Committee will be established, and at the same time, the Southwest Political Affairs Committee and the Southwest Military Branch will be established as three institutions to preside over the important political, military, and party affairs of the Southwest. As for the Central Party Headquarters, which was previously in Guangdong, it has been gradually closing down and is required to complete the closure before the 15th of this month. From the 6th to the 15th of this month, working hours will be increased, so all staff must arrive at the department at 8:00 a.m. every day and will not be dismissed until 8:00 p.m. They will also dine in the department. During the closure period, they may not go out without permission. From this, we can see the busyness of rushing to complete the closure. As for the members of the Southwest Executive Department of the Central Party Headquarters and the Southwest Political Affairs Committee, they have successively taken office. A joint meeting was held on the 5th to discuss various ongoing cases. At 10:00 a.m. on the 6th, another joint meeting was held in the National Government conference hall. Those present included Deng Zhiru, Xiao Focheng, Chen Jitang, Liu Jiwen, Lin Yizhong, Li Xiaosheng, Qu Fangpu, Yang Xiji, and more than ten others. Xiao Focheng presided over the meeting. There was a detailed discussion on the organization of the Southwest Executive Department and the Military Branch, and various items of the Political Affairs Committee. The results of the discussion were as follows: (1) The organizational regulations of the Southwest Executive Department of the Central Party Headquarters were adopted. (2) The organizational regulations of the Southwest Political Affairs Committee were adopted. (3) The principles for the recurring expenses of the above two institutions were determined. In addition, the distribution of new agency staff and the resettlement of comrades who opposed Chiang Kai-shek were decided. The organization of the Southwest Military Branch was largely discussed on that day, but no specific decision was made. The organization of the Southwest Executive Department of the Central Party Headquarters and the Southwest Political Affairs Committee is quite simple. The Executive Department has a Secretariat and an Organization Group, a Publicity Group, and an Overseas Party Affairs Group, which are reorganized from the original Secretariat and three committees of the Central Party Headquarters. The Political Affairs Committee has several departments to manage various political affairs. The institutions of the various provinces in the Southwest that are related to the committee are all under the supervision and command of the committee. The affairs of the above two committees are handled by the Standing Committee members of each committee. (January 7th)

Shantou Party-Student Turmoil Escalates 71

▲ All Schools Completely Strike

Shantou Correspondence: Last year, students in Shantou City had a dispute with the city party headquarters, which led to the suspension of the Anti-Japanese Association and affected the work of resisting Japan and saving the country. The student side insisted that primary school students had the freedom to participate in saving the country and demanded punishment of those suspected of corruption in the former Anti-Japanese Association, as well as a thorough investigation of the China and Foreign Cotton Mill, etc. The party headquarters insisted on severely punishing the students who caused trouble during the patrol on the 15th and preserving the authority of the party. Both sides went to extremes, and the turmoil intensified day by day. The party headquarters of Chaoyang, Chenghai, Chaoan, and Huilai counties have sent telegrams in support of the Shantou City party headquarters. Primary and secondary schools in various counties have also risen up to support the students in Shantou City. The Shantou City Student National Salvation Association has resolved to implement a strike from December 30th and wait for the higher authorities to issue clear instructions. At the same time, it will send personnel to various counties to establish joint associations of student anti-Japanese national salvation in various counties. On the afternoon of the 31st, a strike picket group was formed at the Commercial College. The group stipulated nine members, divided into general affairs, documents, pickets, team leaders, etc., and selected students from the student associations of nine schools, including Gao Zhuan, No. 1 Middle School, Girls' Middle School, Youlian, Lan, Yu Huai, Zhongying, and Minqiang, to jointly organize it. On New Year's Day this year, student teams paraded and promoted anti-Japanese sentiment, and posted slogans. The city party headquarters also posted slogans to eliminate all reactionaries. Now both sides have fortified their positions, and it is not known how to resolve it. (January 4th)

Bandits Withdraw from Huangpi 72

▲ Li Mingzhong Resigns as Border Area Pacification Commissioner

Hankou Correspondence: Kuang Jizhu's department of the Fourth Army of the Red Bandits, with all its strength, captured Huang'an this time and attacked Huangpi, almost threatening Wuhan. It destroyed the Pinghan Railway. He Chengjing, the Pacification Commissioner stationed in Hubei, seeing the rampant banditry, specially dispatched heavy troops to suppress and encircle them in various directions. Xu Tingyao's 11th and 12th Brigades of the Fourth Division were responsible for the front, attacking from Hengdian. Xia Douyin's 13th Division and Xiao Zhichu's 44th Division were responsible for the flanks. Xia's division attacked from Qijiawan, and Xiao's division attacked from Zhujiawan. In addition, the 48th Division's Han Changjun Brigade was responsible for the rear, attacking from Xinjie, Hekou, and Changqu. The 4th Aviation Team dispatched two aircraft to bomb everywhere. The railway artillery team dispatched the 9th Team to patrol the railway. Xu Tingyao was also sent to the front line to supervise the troops. All troops, aircraft, and artillery vehicles were temporarily placed under his command. Xu departed on the 6th and, after arriving at Hengdian, immediately ordered a general offensive. The fighting was fierce on the 6th, 7th, and 8th. The bandits suffered heavy losses due to being attacked from three sides and retreated north. Although the bandits retreated north, they still gathered in large numbers in Changxuanling and Yanzi Gang and built solid fortifications. They could retreat for a long time and then attack again. When Xu's division and Han's brigade launched from Xinjie, Hekou, and Changyan, the bandit army was attacked from both sides and felt increasingly unable to support itself, so it decided to withdraw from Huang'an and, if necessary, flee into Henan Province or detour around northern Hubei and join forces with He Long. It was heard that the withdrawal began on the 9th and was completed by the 11th. The various armies that suppressed and encircled the bandits returned to their garrisons after the bandits had fled far away. Xu Tingyao's division returned to Wuhan completely on the 11th and was stationed in Wuchang and Hankou's Qinjiaji. Huangpi County Town is still defended by Li Mingzhong's 30th Division. It is said that the local area is safe and order has been completely restored. After Li's troops recovered Qiliping in Huang'an last year, they repeatedly confronted the bandits. Now is the time to encourage morale and take the opportunity to attack the bandit dens again, so as to permanently eliminate the bandit scourge in the border area of Henan, Anhui, and Hubei. Unexpectedly, Li suddenly claimed that his lung disease had recurred and that it was difficult to perform his duties. On the 10th, he telegraphed He Yingqin, Minister of Military Administration, and Zhu Peide, Chief of Staff, asking them to request the National Government to relieve him of his duties as Pacification Commissioner of the Henan-Hubei-Anhui Border Area and concurrently as Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in Eastern Hubei, in order to recuperate. Although Li himself went to Huangpi on the 11th to await orders, he still used the 30th Division Commander to search and suppress the remaining bandits, but his attitude was passive, and it was feared that sweeping the dens and plowing the courtyards would not be possible in a short time. It has been found that there are as many as 40,000 bandits remaining in Hubei Province. The damage suffered in Huangpi this time was only part of Xu Xiangqian's force. The main force of the Kuang bandits was not greatly damaged, and it is difficult to avoid a resurgence. (January 11th)

Northwest Flight Success 73

▲ No. 1 Aircraft Returns to Beiping from Tianshan

▲ Li Jingcong Talks About the Flight Experience

Beiping Correspondence: The Eurasia No. 1 aircraft, which was test-flying in the Northwest, returned east the day before yesterday after arriving in Dihua on the 22nd of last month. It stopped at Ruoshui River that night and took off from Ruoshui River yesterday morning (the 9th), passing through Suiyuan without stopping. It flew to Nanyuan, Beiping at 4:25 p.m. The Northwest trip was thus a success. The aircraft is scheduled to be taken by Li Jingcong and others tomorrow to Nanjing and then to Shanghai. After Li reported the test flight to the company, he immediately began to plan the official opening of the route. Yesterday afternoon at 5 p.m., after Li and others returned to the city, the reporter visited the Eurasia Company office. Li kindly talked about his flight experience as follows: [

At 7 a.m. on the 20th of last month, I, along with pilot Luz, Stonemide, Shi Berlin, and others, departed from Nanyuan in the No. 1 aircraft. At 10 a.m., we arrived at Guihua. After stopping to refuel, we flew to Ruoshui River. It was already dusk, and we searched everywhere for the place where we had agreed to place gasoline but could not find it. We circled in the air for about an hour. It was already dark, and we had no choice but to land in an ancient city. The city is named Heichengzi and was built in the Han Dynasty. It has now been buried and no one knows about it. There were no possessions in the city. We curled up in the aircraft. We fired our guns late at night, but no one responded. We could not even hear the sound of dogs. The next day, we waited until noon, but no one came. So we flew up again and discovered a herd of camels in the air. We landed to ask the camel riders and were able to find the place where the gasoline was placed. It was already past noon, and it was too late to fly to Dihua, so we spent another night in Ruoshui River. On the morning of the 22nd, we flew west and safely arrived in Dihua at 2 p.m. At that time, representatives of the Xinjiang Provincial Government and many people had arrived at the scene to welcome us, which was extremely enthusiastic. The whole city also hung flags to mark the celebration. We met with Chairman Jin Shuren five times in Xinjiang. Jin praised the success of the flight and was willing to do his best to help. In addition, he entrusted us to bring more than 100 catties of valuable items to his representatives in Beiping and Tianjin, Guanglu Jun, and other agency personnel. The various agencies also regarded the flight as an unprecedented event and held banquets to welcome us, so our social activities were endless. Dihua City is located north of the Tianshan Mountains. The climate has been quite cold recently. The daytime temperature is below 15 degrees Celsius, and the nighttime temperature is below 20 or 30 degrees Celsius. The city gates close at 4 p.m. every day, and the night is unusually cold. The people there only know news from the interior from two or three months ago. The Beiping and Tianjin newspapers are transported to the area by the Siberian Railway, which takes a month and a half. Those transported from the interior take three months. This time, we brought the Beiping and Tianjin newspapers from the 19th of last month, and the people there treated them as rare treasures, praising them as opening a new era of culture. The local newspaper, Tianshan Daily, only published news from two or three months ago. Now that they had the newspapers we brought, they reprinted as much as possible. Until yesterday, when we left Xinjiang, the newspaper was still using materials from the Beiping and Tianjin newspapers from the 19th. It is a pity that I was unable to bring back a few copies. We originally planned to test-fly to Yili and Tacheng in Dihua, but then temporarily cancelled it. Since we had already stayed in Xinjiang for more than ten days, we decided to return east yesterday morning. We departed at 7 a.m. and arrived at Ruoshui River at 4 p.m., where we spent the night. We took off from Ruoshui River at 7:30 this morning, passed through Guihua without landing, and went straight to Nanyuan. This trip was a risky attempt because we were completely unfamiliar with the geography. The result was that we measured the distance from Beiping to Ruoshui River to be 1,400 kilometers, and the distance from Ruoshui River to Dihua to be 1,200 kilometers, a total of 2,600 kilometers. There were more high mountains along the way than plains. The flight altitude was about 700-800 meters and 2,000-3,000 meters. But we arrived safely and on time, which is gratifying. I am scheduled to take the same aircraft to Nanjing and then to Shanghai the day after tomorrow to report the test flight to the company, so as to prepare for the official opening of the route.] (January 10th)

Chambers of Commerce in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province Request Amendments to the Business Tax Rectification Measures 74

Representatives from the chambers of commerce of various counties in Jiangsu Province went to the Provincial Government's Finance Department on the morning of the 11th to personally submit a petition, requesting the cessation of business tax rectification measures that contain clauses that harass merchants. Chairman Gu and Director Shu of the Finance Department were in Shanghai to discuss the Grand Canal project, so Jin Tigan and Cheng Botang received the representatives separately and promised to forward the petition. The petition is recorded below: [Since the central government abolished likin (internal transit tax), local governments, in order to compensate for the reduced revenue due to the abolition of likin, have implemented business taxes. This measure is a last resort for the provincial governments and is understood by all merchants. However, since its implementation, the chambers of commerce have repeatedly gathered to discuss and request changes to the collection methods, as they are not conducive to business, but these requests have not been adopted by the Provincial Government's Finance Department. As a result, business conditions have not been harmonious, and the measures are largely unsuitable, leading to poor revenue collection after half a year. This is partly due to the impact of floods and financial problems, but also to a lack of communication and cooperation between officials and the public. Now, the provincial government, due to a shortage of tax revenue, has specially formulated thirteen articles for rectification, with the original intention of increasing tax revenue and allowing the provincial treasury to have sufficient funds for operation, which should still be understood by merchants. However, after careful analysis of the articles, the chambers of commerce feel that they are even more incompatible with business conditions and are sufficient to cause harassment, and they violate the regulations of the Ministry of Finance's amended articles, which is unacceptable to merchants. Therefore, we specifically enumerate the following points: For example, Article 5 of the rectification measures states, "This investigation should be entrusted to the bureaus to send personnel to fill out the declaration forms household by household." Article 6 states, "For stores that use business volume as the standard, they should present their business ledgers for the 20th year of the Republic of China during the investigation. For stores that use capital amount as the standard, they should present their business contract documents during the investigation. Those who do not comply with the investigation and presentation will have their ledgers and contracts retrieved and reviewed by the Review Committee for a decision." The above two articles stipulate that, on the one hand, the bureaus should be entrusted to send personnel, and on the other hand, ledgers and contracts should be presented during the investigation, without regard for the provisions of Article 6 of the Ministry of Finance's amended regulations. Article 6 of the Ministry of Finance's amendment stipulates that the collection agency may, when necessary, send personnel to investigate and inspect ledgers, documents, and goods, but must do so in conjunction with the local chamber of commerce. The essence of this article is that everyone knows that sending personnel to investigate and inspect is a method that the collection agency can adopt when necessary, and it is not that the bureaus can send personnel to investigate and inspect at any time or when it is not necessary. Furthermore, even if the collection agency sends personnel to investigate and inspect when necessary, it must do so in conjunction with the local chamber of commerce. This proviso shows that investigation must be done in conjunction with the chamber of commerce. In other words, even if the bureaus want to carry out the investigation independently, they cannot do so. Even according to the Business Tax Law passed by the Legislative Yuan, it only stipulates that businesses should declare the amount of capital and business, and only when the provincial or municipal government considers it inaccurate can the Review Committee review it. The organization of the Review Committee is even more clearly stipulated, that the review committee members representing the interests of taxpayers should not be less than one-third of the total number of committee members. This further shows that the bureaus cannot independently and arbitrarily investigate and inspect. This is the first point that the Department should request to abolish according to the Ministry's regulations and the Business Tax Law. Another example is Article 8 of the rectification measures, "Wholesale and retail are taxed separately," which is not permitted by the Business Tax Law and should be collected uniformly from the 21st year of the Republic of China according to regulations. The Business Tax Law is the general outline stipulated by the central government. As for the detailed implementation rules, the competent officials should supplement them based on the actual situation. Since the Business Tax Law does not stipulate that wholesale and retail must be uniformly treated, and according to the actual situation, the nature of retail and wholesale is indeed different, it is necessary to collect them separately. Moreover, does not the Business Tax Law clearly stipulate in Article 1 of the new measures that the implementation will be postponed again from January of next year? What is shown to the merchants is the postponement of implementation, so it should not be considered whether the Business Tax Law permits it or not. Furthermore, the phrase "collected uniformly from the 21st year of the Republic of China according to regulations" is unclear as to which regulations it refers to, making it impossible to follow. Moreover, Article 14 of the Ministry of Finance's amended regulations has clearly stipulated that wholesale can be taxed at half the business tax rate. It is absolutely clear that separate taxation of wholesale and retail is permitted by Article 14 of the Ministry of Finance's amended regulations. In addition, Article 1 of the new rectification measures passed by the provincial government clearly admits that the tax rates will still be handled in accordance with the regulations of the Ministry of Finance. Since it is said that the regulations of the Ministry of Finance will still be followed, then wholesale and retail should be taxed separately, and wholesale should be taxed at half the rate. Why is it ambiguous and said that it will be "collected uniformly according to regulations," which violates the regulations of the Ministry of Finance? Furthermore, Article 10 of the new measures states, "Since the tax rate is temporarily unchanged, it should be collected in accordance with the original tax rate set by the Ministry of Finance, and no further reduction or circumvention is allowed." It is true that merchants should not be allowed to reduce or circumvent taxes at will, but why can the government freely change or increase the measures it has set in relation to the original regulations of the Ministry of Finance? The above are the important points in the rectification measures that violate the regulations of the Ministry of Finance and contradict the regulations, and should be abolished. This is the second point. Furthermore, Article 13 of the rectification measures states, "The bureau staff who collect taxes can extract 20% of the extra revenue as a reward." Using the surplus or deficit of tax collection as the standard for reward and punishment is originally the general policy of the likin era. Moreover, business tax can only be collected according to the reported amount. Unless there is arbitrary exaction, there is no possibility of extra revenue. The provision of this article is tantamount to opening the door to corruption and harassment, and should be abolished. This is the third point. The above only lists a few points in the new measures that violate the regulations of the Ministry of Finance and are difficult for merchants to agree to. We urgently request the government to suspend the implementation of these measures and convene a meeting of all provincial chambers of commerce within the shortest possible time to properly discuss rectification methods, so as to comply with the principle of public finance. The government's aim is to rectify provincial tax revenue, while the merchants' aim is to protect their own interests. If they can sit together and deliberate carefully, there will be no situation where both cannot be taken into consideration. The chambers of commerce have researched in detail and have the same opinion. We hereby jointly submit this petition for your review and approval. We are filled with anticipation and await your command.]

Local News

Sun Ke Expresses Determination 86

▲ Decision to Organize a Special Committee

▲ To Cope with the Current National Crisis

▲ All Central Committee Members Return to Beijing This Morning Together

Premier Sun Ke’s trip to Fenghua was cancelled. Key figures of the central government, such as Vice Premier Chen Mingshu, Foreign Minister Chen Youren, Interior Minister Li Wenfan, Finance Minister Huang Hanliang, and Railway Minister Ye Gongchuo, left Beijing for Shanghai, causing a virtual standstill in the central political apparatus. Shanghai became the focus of the current situation. Yesterday, these key figures held an important meeting again at Sun’s residence on Molier Road to discuss emergency measures to cope with the national crisis. They decided to organize a special committee as a stopgap measure before Wang Jingwei, Chiang Kai-shek, and Hu Hanmin arrive in Beijing, in order to overcome the current major crises in diplomacy, finance, and military affairs. Premier Sun, believing that a solution to the current situation has been discussed, decided to return to Beijing with all the ministers this morning. Yesterday, Sun also expressed a proactive attitude of “national survival with survival, national demise with demise.”

▲ Establishment of a Special Committee. Yesterday morning at ten o'clock, Sun Ke, Yu Youren, Chen Mingshu, Chen Youren, Li Wenfan, Huang Hanliang, Ye Gongchuo, Zou Lu, Feng Yuxiang, Li Jishen, Li Zongren, Wu Tiecheng, Ma Chaojun, and other key central figures held an important meeting at Sun's residence for two hours. During the meeting, Sun Ke reported on the current difficulties of the government and the tense diplomatic situation. Subsequently, everyone successively expressed their opinions, stating that at this critical moment of national crisis, they could not sit idly by as the central government remained vacant. Therefore, it was decided to establish a special committee under the Central Political Conference to cope with the current serious national issues. The members of the special committee would include Wang Jingwei, Chiang Kai-shek, and Hu Hanmin, the Standing Committee members of the Central Political Conference, as ex officio members, and Sun Ke, Chen Mingshu, He Yingqin, Yu Youren, Chen Youren, Feng Yuxiang, Li Jishen, Li Zongren, Zhu Peide, and nine others would be elected as members. All Central Committee members will return to Beijing today, and the Central Standing Committee meeting will be held tomorrow to formally finalize the decision.

▲ Sun Ke's Remarks Before Returning to Beijing. Premier Sun is scheduled to return to Beijing with all the ministers and Central Committee members at 9:30 this morning. Yesterday, he made the following remarks on the current situation: (Reporter asked) Mr. Chiang, Mr. Hu, and Mr. Wang have not yet confirmed their arrival in Beijing, and you are leaving Beijing at this time, making the central government even more vacant, leading to the standstill of all matters and causing public anxiety. You bear important entrustments from the Party and the country. How will you overcome this difficulty? I believe you have deliberated thoroughly and would like to hear your thoughts. (Answer) The national crisis is becoming increasingly urgent every day, truly an unprecedentedly difficult situation since the founding of the Republic. It cannot be salvaged without gathering the talent and strength of the entire nation. As a member of the public, and especially with a deep and long-standing historical relationship with the Chinese Nationalist Party, I cannot shirk my responsibility at this critical moment. However, considering the recent situation, if the central organs cannot be strengthened, then this kind of past responsibility of the Premier cannot be borne by me. In terms of finance, the debt burden has been mounting for several years, and all resources have been exhausted. The central government's annual revenue is originally 400 to 500 million, but after paying off debts, less than 100 million is available. If we want to issue more public bonds, the collateral has already been completely used up, and the market price of bonds is only 20 to 30 percent of their face value. Even if we forcibly issue public bonds, it will not help. Recently, the government's monthly fiscal revenue is only 6 million, while the expenditure is 18 million for military expenses alone, even after the reductions approved by the previous Finance Committee. Government expenses and education expenses still require 4 million, resulting in a shortfall of 16 million. The national finance has reached such an extreme state of difficulty that even the minimum necessary expenses for maintaining the national organization cannot be supported. This affects various issues such as diplomacy and military affairs. Even with good solutions, they are difficult to implement due to the constraints of the situation. The reason why I decided to go to Fenghua in person the other day to ask Mr. Chiang to return to Beijing quickly, and the reason why the central government also sent Mr. Yu Youren to Hong Kong to urge Mr. Hu to come north immediately, is precisely because the national crisis has reached this point. There is no other way but to do our utmost to facilitate the cooperation of the leaders. For several days in Shanghai, responsible comrades from the central government have repeatedly consulted with each other and expressed agreement with my views. All of them believe that at this time, Chinese Nationalist Party comrades must restore the spirit of revolution, and everyone is willing to sacrifice personal interests in order to address the nation's urgent needs first, and must break through the difficult situation to find a way out for the Party and the country. Before Mr. Hu, Mr. Wang, and Mr. Chiang arrive in Beijing, the central organs especially need urgent measures to strengthen them. Therefore, it was unanimously decided that all Central Committee members remaining in Shanghai will first return to Beijing tomorrow morning, and the Central Standing Committee will establish a special committee within the Central Political Conference to take full responsibility for coping with the national crisis and quickly handling various political affairs. At the same time, we will continue to urge Mr. Hu, Mr. Wang, and Mr. Chiang to come to Beijing as soon as possible to share the great responsibility. Mr. Wang has indicated that he will come to Beijing as soon as he recovers from his illness. Mr. Hu and Mr. Chiang, after such earnest appeals from comrades and the people of the country, should not be able to ignore everything and should be able to comfort the people's ardent hopes. Today is truly the autumn of life and death for the Chinese nation, and it is also the day for us to sacrifice ourselves to serve the country. I firmly believe that as long as the people of the country embrace the spirit of revolution, the affairs of the nation will definitely not be without hope. Today, all the comrades in the central government have made up their minds to share the fate of the nation and resolutely go to Beijing together to jointly take responsibility for the current situation, and there has been a turning point. I will certainly bear my share of the responsibility and will not hesitate to go through fire and water. I hope that all compatriots across the country will also share this determination and work together with the government. Regardless of diplomacy or finance, we must be the government's support. As for the civil and military officials who serve the country, they must work hard and diligently at this time and not seek personal gain. Then, a nation can be revitalized through adversity, and who knows if the enemy's disaster will not be a blessing to us. I especially hope that the news media will promote this idea to the people, so that everyone can shoulder their responsibility to save the country and not just blame the government. This is to do everything possible to save the country, which is the great fortune of the nation."

Yu Youren Goes to Hong Kong 87

▲ Left Shanghai by Ship at Eight O'Clock This Morning

▲ Says the Political Situation Can Develop from Now On

Yu Youren, President of the Control Yuan, representing the central government, went to Hong Kong to urge Mr. Hu Hanmin to go north to jointly take responsibility for the major affairs of the country. Last night, Mr. Yu, accompanied by Secretary-General Wang Luyi, Liu Kaizhong, and others, took a ferry from the Xinguang Wharf to the Puxi Dalai Company Wharf and boarded the President Jackson, scheduled to set sail for Hong Kong at eight o'clock this morning. Before his departure, Mr. Yu told reporters briefly that this trip was to convey the common intention of the central government to persuade Mr. Hu to come to Beijing despite his illness and to explain the intentions of the central government to comrades in Guangdong. He firmly believes that the political situation can develop rapidly from now on, so as to comfort the hopes of the people. The reporter also asked if he had seen Mr. Wang. He replied, "I know that the doctor advised Mr. Wang not to see guests, so I did not go. But I firmly believe that Mr. Wang will go to Beijing immediately when his illness improves slightly."

Opinions on Financial Matters After Provinces Seize Taxes 88

▲ The Consolidated Tax Administration Will Send Personnel to Various Provinces for Investigation

▲ Deputy Finance Minister Lin Kanghou Declines to Take Office Due to the Tax Seizure Issue

Since the establishment of the unified government, provincial governments have suddenly taken the action of seizing customs duties and consolidated taxes, and Guangdong Province has directly collected national taxes and has not yet reported or remitted them to the central government. There are even rumors that Tianjin and other places are also withholding tax revenues. This matter is of great importance to national finance and bond credit. A reporter from the Huadong News Agency inquired with the authorities of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Finance and the Consolidated Tax Administration yesterday. According to the Ministry of Finance, when the unified government was not yet established, Guangdong Province had indicated that after the establishment of the government, national taxes in Guangdong Province would still be collected by the central government. However, after the unified government was established, Guangdong Province did not fulfill this commitment, and the provinces of Shandong and Fujian also followed suit. There are also confirmed plans in North China provinces to seize salt taxes, etc. Previously, the central government's tax revenue reached 30 million per month, but now it has suddenly decreased to 6 million, while the monthly military expenditure requires 18 million, and administrative and educational expenses amount to 4 million, leaving no solution. Deputy Finance Minister Lin Kanghou has therefore delayed taking office. This situation has the potential to cause the national finance to completely collapse. The reporter then visited the Consolidated Tax Administration. According to the section chief of the administration, it is a fact that various provinces are seizing consolidated taxes. This action has a significant impact on the consolidated tax treasury bond fund. Currently, Director Zou has just taken office, and everything within the department is still being reorganized. Once the reorganization is completed, personnel will be sent to various provinces for investigation and to communicate with various provincial governments.

Lin Kanghou has not yet taken office nearly ten days after the government appointed him as the Permanent Secretary of the Ministry of Finance. Reporters specifically visited him at the Bank Association at 3 p.m. yesterday. After Mr. Lin invited them to sit down and exchanged pleasantries, they began their conversation. (Reporter asked) When will you go to Nanjing to take office? (Mr. Lin replied) I plan not to take office. (Asked) Why did you agree to take office initially? (Answer) This time, the government invited people from the public to take on national affairs. All citizens should take on this responsibility without regard to sacrifice. Moreover, the people in the current government do not agree with the policies of the previous government and want to innovate and start anew with the people. Therefore, I agreed to consider taking on the position after a definite direction was decided. (Asked) What are the reasons why you plan not to take office? (Answer) Everyone knows that the government's finances have reached a dead end. Now, to overcome the difficulties, first, the military must realize the need to reduce military spending and, at the same time, use the military to protect production; second, various provinces must maintain the central government's financial unity and not seize national taxes in order to maintain the bond fund, so that the nation's credit will not be lost and public bonds can be reissued to carry out industrial and transportation construction. However, at the beginning of the new government's establishment, Guangdong Province was the first to refuse to return the national taxes seized previously to the central government and continued to seize them. Then, Shandong and other provinces followed suit. Recently, there have been rumors that the northern provinces are also seizing customs duties and salt taxes. That is, the provinces not only do not realize the need to reduce military spending but also seize the central government's revenue, indirectly robbing the public bond fund. On the one hand, they receive salaries, and on the other hand, they seize revenue, which is no different from increasing military spending. In this situation, I believe that it is hopeless to seek financial innovation from the government. Therefore, there is no need to hold a false title and help oppress the people. (Asked) Does that mean you will not be involved in financial matters at all? (Answer) I am willing to work with the people to strive for financial innovation. The people are well aware that over the past few years, tens of thousands of yuan of public bonds have been issued and used for military expenses. Previous financial authorities have repeatedly proposed reductions, but they could not be implemented. Today, 18 million yuan is still required each month, and what the military repays to our people is only internal warfare, bandits, communists, and opium. However, the authorities still tell the people that if they want to quell internal warfare, eliminate the communists, and eliminate bandits, they must raise more military expenses; otherwise, they will not be responsible for the people's suffering. Therefore, the people squeeze out every last drop of blood and sweat to survive. How can the people survive in this situation of utter devastation? If the people of all provinces and regions do not rise up together to supervise the finances, then politics will never be clear and the national crisis cannot be saved. The reporter, seeing that Mr. Lin had many visitors, arranged for another conversation and shook hands to say goodbye.

Continued Opposition to the Seizure of National Taxes 89

▲ Banking and Money Industry Association Fund

▲ Sends Telegrams to Various Authorities

▲ Remittance of Tax Revenues to the Central Government

The Shanghai Banking and Money Industry Association and the Treasury Bond Fund Custody Committee telegraphed the central government and various authorities yesterday regarding the seizure of customs duties and salt taxes by various parties, appealing to them. The original telegram is as follows:

▲ Two Associations of the Banking and Money Industry

▲ Telegram to the National Government's Executive Yuan, Nanjing. Revered Executive Yuan of the Nanjing National Government: Recently, news of various provinces seizing national taxes has been widely reported. If this is true, it is truly shocking. Salt and customs taxes are used to guarantee foreign debts. If there is any breach of contract, it will inevitably lead to reproaches from foreigners. At this time of national peril and urgent diplomacy, we fear that it will give enemy countries an excuse and lose the sympathy of friendly countries. The situation is very important. This is one reason why it is unacceptable from the perspective of the diplomatic situation. The way to establish a nation is to prioritize good faith. The current tobacco, alcohol, stamp, consolidated, customs, and salt taxes are all funds for public bonds and treasury bonds, which are managed by associations and recorded in regulations. If the fund is shaken, the bonds will become worthless. If one province sets a bad example, other provinces will follow suit, and national credit will be lost. In the future, the central and local governments will have no source of funds for emergency needs or for daily construction. This is the second reason why it is unacceptable from the perspective of the financial future. The government has frequently taken out loans over the years, and the people trust the government. Most of the loose capital has gathered, so there are holders of bonds all over the country. If the bonds lose credibility one day, the domestic financial system will inevitably be disrupted, and the livelihoods of ordinary people will be destroyed. The harm is unimaginable. This is the third reason why it is unacceptable from the perspective of the national economy. The matter is important, and the associations cannot remain silent. In addition to sending telegrams to the authorities in Beiping, Shandong, Hubei, and Guangdong, we respectfully request that you order a strict prohibition to demonstrate unification and care for the people's livelihood. We await your orders with trepidation. The Shanghai Banking and Money Industry Association, respectfully.

We hope that you will not seize all customs and salt taxes in the northern provinces in order to avoid shaking the foundations of the country. It would be fortunate for the nation and fortunate for the people. The Shanghai Banking and Money Industry Association, respectfully.

It would be fortunate for the nation and fortunate for the people. (Same title as above)

The Bank of China Increases the Reserve for Banknote Issuance 90

▲ All Domestic Bonds Whose Market Prices Have Fallen Are Excluded

▲ Banknote Holders Can Rest Easy

Since the public disclosure of banknote issuance by the Bank of China, its credibility has been evident. Recently, because a portion of the guarantee reserve consisted of domestic bonds whose market prices have fallen, the people had doubts. It has now been decided that these domestic bonds will be excluded from the reserve in the future in order to strengthen it. This demonstrates that the bank's operations are stable and take into account the overall financial situation. The letter from the bank to the Public Inspection Committee is recorded below: We take the maintenance of a strong reserve for all our bank notes. Sixty percent of it is composed of cash, while the other forty percent is composed of guarantee fund of gold bond from domestic or international locations, and commercial draft. The recent drop in bond prices has had an unfortunate effect on public perception. Even though we value the guarantee fund in the reserve at the current market value to accurately reflect the financial state, the current situation is still unsatisfactory to our standards. We have decided, starting from the inspection on the fourteenth of this month, to withdraw those bonds whose value has not stabilized and replace them with gold debt bond from domestic or international locations, and commercial draft to stabilize the fund and demonstrate our credibility. The details are as follows: The forty percent reserve fund consists of (1) Domestic debt (A) secured by German and Russian compensations (i) seven-year term bond of face value 22,020.00, market value 13,212.00 (13,000 yuan) (ii) fourteen-year 8% bond of face value 165,000.00, market value 132,000.00 (132,000 yuan) (iii) seventeen-year short term financing bond of face value 3,650,000.00, market value 3,285,000.00 (3,285,000 yuan) (2) Gold bond (A) Sino-Belgium gold bond of face value USD 574,400.00, market value 1,450,505.00 national currency (1,450,505 yuan) (B) Sino-France gold bond of face value USD 907,100.00, market value 2,290,656.56 national currency (2,290,656 yuan 56 cents) (C) UK gold war reparations bond of face value GBP 906,900.00, market value 7,557,500.00 national currency (7,557,500 yuan) (D) Australian dollar gold bond of face value USD 48,000.00, market value 202,020.20 national currency (200,202 yuan 20 cents) (E) Japanese dollar gold bond of face value USD 150,000.00, market value 458,754.21 national currency (458,754 yuan 21 cents) (F) UK gold bond of face value GBP 150,000.00, market value 1,750,000.00 national currency (1,750,000 yuan) (3) Land titles (land titles of properties in Shanghai foreign concession) 12,905,825.21 (12,905,825 yuan 21 cents) (4) Highest grade US stocks USD 760,744.87, market value 3,201,788.87 national currency (5) commercial draft of 3,809,017.14 yuan (3,090,017 yuan and 14 cents) The grand total is 31,715,629 yuan 19 cents. The amount issued on the 11th of this month was 122,351,055 yuan. In addition to the 29,368,124 yuan that the other banks took in notes, the amount issued by our bank was 92,669,231 yuan, and forty percent of the amount is 37,067,692.40 yuan. There is in addition, 11,413 yuan and 21 cents extra. We announce that all the reserve fund is of sufficient amount and kindly request that the Shanghai Bank of China note reserve funds public inspection committee prepare this for review. Thank you. Shanghai Bank of China.

Page 10

Record of the Inauguration of the New Mint Director 91

▲Xu Jiqing Hopes to Abolish Taels and Adopt the Yuan

The newly appointed director of the mint, Mr. Xu Jiqing, arrived at the factory yesterday to take over. A brief account of his inauguration is recorded below: Yesterday at 10:30 a.m., Mr. Xu arrived at the factory. All the factory staff and workers welcomed him. The ceremony hall was set up on the second floor, and the ceremony was carried out accordingly. Then, Mr. Xu delivered a speech, stating that in the eighth and ninth years of the Republic, the banking industry generally believed that the currency system was closely related to finance and should be reorganized. The first step was to abolish taels and use the yuan. The key to abolishing taels and using the yuan lies in the establishment of a mint. At that time, I was also one of the strongest advocates. In the tenth year of the Republic, the Shanghai Mint was established with a loan from a banking syndicate. On March 2nd of that year, the syndicate signed a contract with the government to borrow 2.5 million yuan, and the government would allocate 70,000 yuan per month from the salt surplus, which was expected to be repaid in May of the twelfth year. At the same time, directors Zhong and Sa successively engaged in preparation, purchasing machinery, constructing factory buildings, and hiring the famous American technician, Mr. He Weide, to plan everything. However, the government failed to fulfill the contract and repay the loan on a monthly basis. As a result, the loan was exhausted, and the budget was still insufficient. The factory building was completed, but the machinery had not yet been installed. The Beijing government could not repay the loan and left the factory affairs unattended. Fortunately, the syndicate temporarily kept it safe. By the summer of the sixteenth year of the Republic, the National Government established its capital in Nanjing and paid great attention to the reorganization of the currency system. It appointed Wang Zisong and Tang Shoumin as directors successively. In June of the seventeenth year of the Republic, the Economic Conference resolved that the abolition of taels and the use of the yuan must be completed. Finance Minister Song of Shanghai also tried his best to maintain it. Finally, in that year, the previous debt was completely cleared, and the name was changed to the Central Mint. In October, Guo Biao was appointed as the director and actively carried out the work, specially sending several technicians to Europe and the United States to inspect and add the latest machinery, so that it could become the only mint in the world. Recently, the technicians have returned to China one after another and are actively carrying out the work. Unfortunately, Director Guo passed away due to heart disease on January 3rd of the new year, which is a pity for the future of the mint. Recently, Finance Minister Huang believed that the relationship between the mint and the Central Bank was very close. After I was entrusted with the position of Vice President of the Central Bank and Acting President, I was further ordered to concurrently serve as the Director of the Central Mint. I have always served in the bank and have never been an official. However, the mint has a great relationship with finance. Currently, there is only one minting institution in Hangzhou. In the future, when the goal of abolishing taels and using the yuan is achieved, the urgent need for the Central Mint to start operation goes without saying. I and the banking community have tried our best to advocate in the past, and after the planning of Minister Song and Director Guo, I am optimistic about its success. However, before the establishment of the National Government, the political situation was unstable and undecided, and it has been shelved for a long time. In the past three or four years, although the factory foundation has been solid, it has not been able to start minting because the currency standard of our country has not yet been determined. After the publication of the Kemmerer Report, there has been no concrete plan. Recently, the gold standard of various countries in the world has been shaken, and the United Kingdom has taken the lead in suspending the gold standard, and Japan has followed suit in prohibiting the export of cash. It is expected that the issue of the currency standard will eventually be resolved. The abolition of taels and the use of the yuan and the establishment of a standard system in our country are urgent. If the political situation can be stabilized from now on, the minting of silver coins will be realized, and the mission of the Central Mint can be completed. As for the original staff of this factory, they are all knowledgeable and experienced, so there is no need to make any changes. I hope that my colleagues will work with peace of mind. Afterwards, the guest Mr. Dai Ailu delivered a speech, stating that the currency chaos in our country has a great impact on the national economic life, so the unification of the currency system lies first in abolishing taels and changing to yuan, and the abolition of taels and changing to yuan lies first in completing the Central Mint. Today, when Director Xu took office, he repeatedly told the colleagues of the factory about this hope that he would start work as soon as possible to achieve the goal of unifying the currency system, which would be beneficial to the people's livelihood. After the speech, the slogans "Long live the Republic of China" and other slogans were shouted, and the ceremony ended. After the inauguration ceremony, Mr. Xu briefly talked about the factory affairs with Mr. He Weide, the chief engineer of the factory, and received the secretary and section chief to review several official documents. Then, Chief Engineer He led the tour of the entire factory.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sent Letters to Various Industries Soliciting Opinions on the Strike 92

▲Silk and Satin Industry Vetoed

Yesterday, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent letters to various industries, announcing and soliciting opinions on the student representatives' request for a strike. The letter said: To the esteemed members of the industry, due to the fall of Jinzhou and the Japanese army's advance on Shanhaiguan, the government has no way to deal with it. The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of university students and middle school students in this city has sent representatives to the chamber on the 4th, 5th, 6th, and 7th of this month to request a strike and participate in the citizens' assembly to urge the government to send troops immediately. The chairman of the chamber personally received and explained everything, and submitted it to the 78th Standing Committee meeting for discussion. It was decided that the National Government should be immediately informed by telegram to quickly determine a major plan to use force to recover the lost land and implement revolutionary diplomacy. The issue of a strike is of great importance and should be discussed in detail by the Executive Committee. After the decision was made, in addition to issuing a public telegram, which has been published in various newspapers, the 22nd Executive Committee was convened at 4 p.m. on the 9th of this month to specifically discuss the case. A total of 11 executive committee members and 7 supervisory committee members attended. During the meeting, in addition to the chairman reporting on the progress, the student representatives explained the reasons for advocating a strike and requested (1) that the strike be held on the 11th of this month and (2) that they be allowed to participate in the citizens' assembly on the 17th. After detailed discussions by the committee members present, it was decided that the Executive Supervisory Committee of the chamber would express deep sympathy and admiration for the student representatives' patriotic enthusiasm. The request to participate in the citizens' assembly on the 17th would be notified to all members to actively participate. As for the strike on the 11th, the Executive Supervisory Committee could express its acceptance, but the matter was of great importance and the consent of the various trade associations must be obtained. The date of the strike is proposed to be held on the 17th of this month. Therefore, this case is specially recorded and notified to be handled accordingly. Please promptly reply by letter before the 15th of this month whether or not you agree to hold a strike on the 17th of this month to serve as a basis for the decision. We look forward to your reply and wish you all the best.

In addition, the Shanghai Silk and Satin Trade Association specially replied to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce regarding the student representatives' request for a strike, expressing its veto. The letter said: We hereby reply that we received your letter on January 11th, in which the student representatives, due to the fall of Jinzhou and the Japanese army's advance on Shanhaiguan, proposed to strike and hold a citizens' assembly on the 17th of this month to urge the government to send troops immediately. We were asked whether we agreed and whether we would participate in the assembly. We were informed that the matter was of great importance and that an emergency meeting was immediately convened to submit it for discussion. Everyone said that while sympathy could be expressed for the patriotic actions of the student representatives, the end of the year is approaching, and all businesses must settle their accounts in order to facilitate turnover. If a strike is held at this time, the capital will inevitably be disrupted and fall into stagnation, leading to commercial panic. Although it is not a pity to sacrifice for the country, in the end, it will not only be of no help to the facts, but will also give the reactionaries an opportunity to make trouble, and the violent Japanese invaders will not be affected by it. For the sake of the present, we can only appeal to the National Government to quickly determine a major plan to implement revolutionary diplomacy and invoke the League of Nations Covenant to arouse the justice of various countries. On the one hand, please immediately deploy capable troops to recover the lost land by force, and order the defending officers to be responsible for the survival of the city. In addition to economic sanctions, the people in the rear must firmly maintain their composure and serve as the government's support. Do not panic and make unnecessary sacrifices to expose their weakness and hasten their demise. Therefore, the members of the association believe that suicide is absolutely unacceptable. In addition to sending representatives to participate in the citizens' assembly at the time, the reply was based on the consensus of the members of the association. We respectfully request your esteemed chamber to base your decision on the opinions of the members of the association, promptly sign and reply to the student representatives, consider carefully, withdraw the previous proposal, and seek other appropriate methods. Please also send a telegram to the National Government to quickly determine a major plan to secure the country and resist foreign aggression, and recover the lost land as soon as possible to reassure the people. We look forward to your reply.

Establishment of the Huai Xu Hai National Defense Support Association 96

▲Advocating Training Local Soldiers to Resist Japan

Chen Yanfu, Jiang Jiechao, Dong Bingnan, Ji Qunqing, and other fellow villagers from Jiangsu Xuhai in Shanghai, believe that the land of Huai Xu Hai is an important part of the national defense. Based on historical facts, it is necessary to strengthen the defense. They specially joined with fellow villagers to form the Jiangsu Huai Xu Hai National Defense Support Association, which was established yesterday and issued a declaration stating: The eastern provinces have fallen, and the Japanese bandits are deepening. Diplomacy cannot save the disaster, and military force cannot rush to the border. The integrity of the country is in danger. The people of our Huai Xu Hai live near the port of Haizhou and the Longhai Railway line. During the Ming Dynasty, Japanese pirates once used this route to go south and ravaged more than a dozen coastal provinces for hundreds of years. Finally, Hu Zongxian and Qi Jiguang trained local soldiers to eliminate them. At the beginning of the invasion of the eastern provinces, warships were repeatedly sent to spy on Haizhou to measure its strategy. They wanted to go west along the Longhai Railway line to horizontally impact China's waist and ribs, so that the north and south would lose contact and achieve the effect of individual strikes and encirclement. On the one hand, Haizhou is used as a base to benefit from its fish and salt to supplement its military supplies. The art of war says that [winning the enemy and becoming stronger] is also. The people of our Huai Xu Hai are inherently strong, tolerant of hardship, and have great talents. Since the 20th year of the Republic of China, although the military and bandits have repeatedly multiplied, the people have been overwhelmed. However, ordinary families have purchased self-defense firearms, and young scholars who have shooting skills are estimated to be more than 200,000 in the 18 counties of the three prefectures, and the police teams of each county do not have artillery weapons. If it is possible to transform the scattered into the whole, and use the Weiji Guang and Yu Dayou's methods of defending against Japanese pirates, and learn from Zeng Wenzheng and Zuo Wenxiang's methods of training the group, it can be used to protect against disasters and defend the people. It is generally agreed that soldiers are stationed in agriculture, which is the plan of the past dynasties in our country. Now, the 3.6 million square miles and 28 million people in Liaodong have been captured by the Japanese pirates at their fingertips. Men are used as guns, women are used as the lower ranks, property is confiscated, and national sovereignty is taken away. If the large groups had been united earlier to gather self-defense, the whole to resist Japanese slaves would have led to such a loss of power and humiliation. However, the Japanese slaves are not satisfied with the loss of Liaoning. Once they land from Haizhou, this tragedy will continue the Ming Dynasty and open the prelude. The lessons of the past can be learned. At this critical moment, we should plan ahead. The comrades are specifically organizing themselves to support the national defense and do their best. We specially declare this to the people of the whole country.

Chairman Zhu Zhilin reported on the crew members' request for year-end double salaries, the strike, and Commissioner Guo's resignation. It was immediately decided that (1) a telegram would be sent to the National Government to retain Commissioner Guo, and (2) Zhu Zhilin and twelve others would be assigned to draft and issue the telegram tomorrow morning.

▲Bureau's Statement: A reporter from Xin Sheng News visited the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to inquire about the truth of the four agreed-upon conditions for resolving the strike, which were published in the newspaper. The person in charge of the bureau said that the four conditions reported were proposed by the crew members to the mediators for discussion, and the bureau has not expressed any position on them.

▲Filing for Record: The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Crew Members' Double Salary Petition Group yesterday reported the mediation process to the Shanghai Municipal Government, the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department, the Social Affairs Bureau, the Ministry of Transportation, and the Shanghai Maritime Administration Bureau, requesting approval for filing.

Important Shipping News 106

▲ **Japanese Vessel Mishap:** The Japanese vessel "Asabo-Maru," en route from [unknown] to [unknown] via [unknown] ocean route, sailing at 130 degrees 40 minutes East longitude, 33 degrees 50 minutes North latitude, near a place called Koryo Island, encountered a severe storm and fog. The ship's hull struck a reef and sent out an SOS distress signal. The Japanese Army immediately dispatched the transport vessel "Woosung No. 9" carrying a large quantity of military supplies to Fengtian, to provide assistance upon receiving the news. Subsequently, the Taikoo liner "Taming" also received the signal and sailed to the scene to help with the rescue. Seven passengers and two crew members were rescued on the spot and transferred to the Japanese vessel "Woosung No. 9." The hull of "Asabo-Maru" remains stuck on the reef.

Coal Industry Groups Sanction Yongchang Coal Company 109

▲ **Privately Importing Japanese Coal and Undermining the Anti-Japanese Movement**

▲ **Fellow Business Owners and Workers Unanimously Decide to Sever Ties**

▲ **Public Assembly Resolution** On January 12th, at 2 PM, the Coal Industry Association held a joint meeting of the Executive Committee and Inspection Committee regarding the owner of Yongchang Coal Company (Chihama Bridge, Xinzha Road), Wu Jichang, who on the 11th of this month dispatched store employees with a single manifest for 188 tons of Matsuura coal imported from Mitsui Coal Depot's Kahoto Mine, openly and privately transporting it to the Chihama Bridge warehouse. The inspection staff of this industry encountered them and reported to the inspection staff of the Shanghai Anti-Japanese Association, who together went to seal the coal. Wu Jichang, the owner of Yongchang Coal Company, dared to collude with a Westerner from a certain foreign firm to falsely report to the Gordon Road Police Station that robbers were stealing coal. The police station, acting on the report, dispatched a police car to arrest the alleged robbers. At that time, 5 PM, the inspection staff transferred the Japanese coal from the river to the Yitaixing West Warehouse. The police went to the second branch of the fourth district to demand the extradition of the five inspectors Yan Bin, Ye Yongfu, Fang Bainian, Xie Baoxing from the labor union, and Tang Rongsheng from the Anti-Japanese Association. He Bumming, the chief of the second branch of the fourth district, refused. Later, the association sent a letter and dispatched Pan Yisan and Wang Wenzheng as representatives to provide bail. Twenty-three committee members and over one hundred sixty members attended the meeting, and they publicly elected Wei Hongwen as chairman. The resolutions were: ㈠ How to handle Yongchang's private import of Japanese coal? The meeting resolved: (甲) Announce in the newspaper that Wu Jichang, the owner of Yongchang Coal Company, is guilty of privately buying Japanese coal and undermining the anti-Japanese movement, and send a letter to the banking and money exchange industries requesting them to sever ties with the traitorous merchant Wu Jichang of Yongchang immediately and refuse to list his products on the market. (乙) All businesses in the industry will completely sever ties with Yongchang. (丙) Appoint Lu Qisheng, Pan Yisan, and Mao Chunpu to urge the Anti-Japanese Association to actively handle this case. (丁) Everyone should sever ties with Yongchang, and those who outwardly comply but secretly disobey will be treated the same as Yongchang. ㈡ How to handle Yongchang's false report to the Gordon Road Police Station about coal robbery? The meeting resolved to send a letter to the Public Works Department and the Gordon Road Police Station stating that the association is conducting patriotic movement inspections and requesting that they not misunderstand and believe false reports in the future. On one hand, the association will appoint its perennial legal counsel to file a lawsuit according to law to protect the association's inspectors. An interim proposal was made to reward those who report private imports of Japanese coal. The meeting resolved to award the reporter one yuan per ton, regardless of whether they are in the same industry. The meeting adjourned at 5 PM.

▲ **Labor Union Resolution** The Coal and Firewood Workers' Union held an emergency meeting yesterday, chaired by Zheng Xiaotang, with Yao Suikai as the recorder. ㈠ The chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting and the process of the union dispatching staff to work with the Coal Industry Association to detain a large batch of Japanese goods privately imported by Yongchang Coal Company. ㈡ Yongchang Coal Company's private import of Japanese goods is deliberate sabotage of the patriotic movement and is extremely despicable. How should we express our opinion? The meeting decided to order all workers of the company to resign voluntarily. ㈢ After the resignation, how should the livelihood problems of these workers be solved? The meeting decided that the union should create a list and earnestly request the industry association to take responsibility. ㈣ Notify all workers in the city to never work for Yongchang. The resolution was passed. ㈤ Yongchang Coal Company does not know it is wrong but has detained the union's investigators. How should we handle it? The meeting decided to request higher authorities to handle it strictly and send a letter of warning from the union. ㈥ Should the union send representatives to attend the industry association's hearing? The meeting decided to appoint Zheng Xiaotang and Yao Suikai. ㈦ Restore the union's anti-Japanese work. The resolution was passed.

Japanese Yarn Case Not Yet Heard 110

▲ **Further Investigation Needed Before Decision**

It was reported in this newspaper that the Shenxin Yarn Factory recently uncovered a large batch of Japanese yarn impersonating its "Human Clock" trademark, and the Public Security Bureau, together with the Harbin police, escorted the case to the First Special District Court. This case was originally scheduled to be heard yesterday, but because the court wanted to understand the truth, the police are currently conducting a detailed investigation to allow them to file a public prosecution. Therefore, the hearing was not held yesterday. The Shenxin Yarn Factory has entrusted attorneys Wu Linkun and others from the Tongren Law Firm to handle the case. It is reported that if the police do not file a public prosecution in this case, Shenxin will file a private prosecution. It is now heard that during the investigation yesterday, clues were obtained regarding the exclusive sale of this counterfeit yarn. It is rumored that the crime site is in the French Concession, so the date of the trial is currently difficult to schedule. Because this case is quite significant, it must be thoroughly investigated before a hearing can be held.

It is also heard that the Shenxin Textile Company previously suspected of mixing Japanese goods with the 20-count and 42-count "Human Clock" yarn found on the market and offered a large reward in the newspaper to clarify the matter. Since the case has been solved, it has been proven that this act was entirely the initiative of Japanese merchants to repackage. Therefore, attorney Wu Linkun and others have been entrusted to publish a notice in the newspaper to revoke the previous reward advertisement.

Wu Nanpu Kidnapping: Ransom of 400,000 Demanded 111

▲ **Rescued in the Beixinjing Area**

▲ **Bandits Still Deviously Attempt to Deny Involvement**

▲ **Police Request Investigation of Case**

▲ **Court Hearing Rescheduled for Two Weeks**

Wu Ze, also known as Nanpu, a broker from the Shanghai Yarn and Cloth Exchange, No. 49, is from Gu'an, Jiangxi Province, and is currently 56 years old. He resides at No. 42 Liaoyang Road, Wader Road. On the morning of the 7th of this month, at 9:00 AM, Wu was riding in his private car from his home, intending to go to Linqing Road, Yangshupu, when suddenly multiple kidnappers blocked his path near Pingliang Road and Lan Road, threatening him with guns. They kidnapped Wu and sped away in a black sedan that was waiting by the roadside. After his family learned of this, they reported to the police and requested a rescue. On the 9th, Wu's family suddenly received a letter from the kidnappers demanding a ransom of 400,000 yuan, so they again reported to the police. In the afternoon of the day before yesterday, Lu Liankui, the chief Chinese detective of the General Inspectorate of the General Police Department, received a tip that a person from Tongzhou named Lu Wenbin was the mastermind of this case and was currently hiding in the Suzhou Inn at No. 810 Zhejiang Road. Chief Detective Lu immediately led Chinese detectives Liu Shaokui, Tang Jian, Wu Changkai, detective Feng Zhiming, and Western detective Thanerfou to the inn. They arrested Lu Wenbin in room 24 and also arrested an accomplice named Zhang Afu, taking them both back to the police station. He assigned detectives to guard the room. After strict interrogation of Lu Wenbin, the suspect confessed that the hostage Wu Nanpu was hidden in a bungalow near Fangjia Wood Bridge at the end of Beibaoxing Road, Beixinjing, in the Chinese district. Chief Detective Lu then led Detective Liu, along with detectives Wang Chengying, Bao Han Zhang, Shen Tianbao, Xie Futang, and others, each equipped with weapons, and took Lu Wenbin in a car to the Sixth District Police Station. They went to the address with the police detectives. They arrived at the bandits' den at 2:30 AM. They broke into the house and arrested two people from Tongzhou, Zhang Tonggen and Zhang Laigen. They seized a pistol and five bullets and rescued the hostage Wu Nanpu. They then captured three more people, Lu Maoqing, Zhang Dexing, and Liu Degui, in the next room and took them back to the police station together. The detectives guarding the Suzhou Inn also arrested Sun Jinpeng (also known as Lao Wu) and escorted them to the police station. Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, they were escorted to the Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Judge Zhou Hanting and Prosecutor Qian Hongye took their seats for interrogation. The police lawyer Li Zhishan stated the case and said that the police were prosecuting according to Articles 1 and 2 of the Regulations for the Punishment of Bandits. Due to time constraints, he requested that the hearing be postponed for two weeks to facilitate the investigation. Chinese and Western detectives then reported on the arrest situation. Wu Nanpu then reported on the kidnapping situation and identified Lu Wenbin as the one who held the ransom letter and ordered him to write it in his own handwriting. Zhang Afu was formerly a car driver at the Xinchanglong Customs Broker at No. 287 De'an Lane, North Suzhou Road, and he also had a business account at the agency, so Zhang knew him. This case may have been his tip-off. Sun Jinpeng was the one who carried out the kidnapping on the scene, stripped him of his coat, and stole 36 yuan in cash. Zhang Tonggen, Zhang Laigen, and Lu Maoqing were the bandits who guarded him. Liu Degui was the one who delivered tea and rice to him every day. Lu Wenbin confessed that someone surnamed Ding ordered him to write the draft of the letter, and he did not participate in the prior planning. Zhang Afu denied any involvement in the case. Sun Jinpeng confessed without hesitation. Zhang Tonggen, Zhang Laigen, and Lu Maoqing confessed that Sun Jinpeng ordered them to guard the hostage. Liu Degui confessed to guarding the garden outside the bandits' den and denied delivering tea and rice. The court judge reviewed the confessions and decided to reschedule the case for two weeks and remand all defendants.

Jianghai Customs Burns Confiscated Drugs 113

▲ **Total Value Over 194,000 Silver Dollars**

The Jianghai Customs Anti-Smuggling Team has recently confiscated over thirty loads of prohibited opium in various ships at this port in the past three months. Therefore, the Supervisory Office notified various agencies to hold a burning ceremony yesterday morning in front of the Guanzhan gate at the Chunjiang Wharf, Lujiazui, Pudong. Representatives from the Supervisory Office, Lu Youchang; the Garrison Headquarters, Ye Liangguang; the Municipal Government, Xu Shaoxiu; the First District Court, Ju Zhijing; the Municipal Party Department, Chen Han Jian; the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Wu Weidian; the Anti-Drug Association, Zhou Chucai; and Zhang, the director of the third district of the Public Security Bureau, dispatched a platoon of armed police to maintain order at the site. The Westerner Roberts, from the shipping department of the Customs, and customs officer Huang Yaofu ordered the cooks to simultaneously ignite two or three kilns. After the various drugs were verified and the numbers were confirmed, the burning began at 9:00 AM and was completed at noon. A total of 35 loads, 88 catties, 8 taels, and 5 qian of opium were destroyed, valued at 153,332.8 yuan. In addition, 674.5 taels of morphine, heroin, etc. were valued at 33,725 yuan. Other narcotics were valued at 7,178.3 yuan, smoking paraphernalia were valued at 264.75 yuan, and poppy husks were valued at 229.7 yuan. The total value of the above drugs was over 194,730 silver dollars, which is truly frightening to hear.
