Mastermind of Kidnapping Case Three Years Ago Identified 116

▲ **Huang Xianwu Tragically Torn to Pieces**

▲ **Shi Danran Confesses to Past Events**

The notorious bandit Shi Danran, also known as Danquan, 28 years old, from Shaoxing, specializes in colluding with gangs to kidnap people for ransom and tear up tickets in this city, and there are too many cases to count. Recently, he was arrested by the police in the French Concession for another kidnapping case and sent to the court, where he was sentenced to five years in prison and then sent to the mainland for legal action. Recently, Dong Mingde, a foreman from the First District of Nanshi, reported through an informant that Shi was the mastermind of the kidnapping of Huang Xianwu, the owner of Huang Yitai Longan Store in Xian Gua Street, outside the Dadongmen of Nanshi, in the Republic of China in 1928. Yesterday morning, he took detective Yuan Haishan, Lu Anpu, and others to the court to extradite Shi and interrogated him in Nanshi. According to him, in January of the Republic of China in 1928, he met Zhou Zuohan, a former battalion commander, at a friend's house. Both sides talked about how it would be better to do some business since they had been idle for a long time. Then, Chen Bolin, as an informant, came up with the idea of kidnapping Huang Xianwu, the owner of Huang Yitai Longan Store in Xian Gua Street, outside the Dadongmen. So, on the morning of the second day of the second lunar month of that year, around 8:00 AM, Zhou Zuohan assigned Zhou Afa, Wang Jinshi, and someone named Youbing to carry firearms, and Ma Guisheng drove a car near the Dadongmen and kidnapped Huang Xianwu and hid him on the floor of a building at a certain number on Hou Chang Road, Yu Garden Road, North City, and Zhou and others guarded the hostage. He then wrote a letter and sent it to Huang's family demanding a ransom. Huang's family sent their friend Wang Huiru, also known as Wang Laowu, to meet with Qiu Bosun, the person assigned by him, at the Central Hotel in North Shanghai, and they met several times. Unexpectedly, Wang had bad intentions and not only did not take the money to redeem the ticket but continued to embezzle more than 4,000 yuan in foreign currency. He was extremely angry and tore up the ticket. At that time, he shot Huang Xianwu to death with a pistol. Chen Bolin, Zhou Afa, Wang Jinshi, and others are all on the run. Zhou Zuohan, Ma Guisheng, and others have been arrested and executed by firing squad in other kidnapping cases. He said that since the matter concerned kidnapping, he was ordered to prepare a document and submit it to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Train Passenger Dies Tragically on Wasteland 117

▲ **Wife and Children Cry Piteously**

▲ **Kind Villagers Help With Arrangements**

A Jing-Hu train departed from Beijing the day before yesterday and arrived at Nanxiang Station around 3:00 PM. A passenger, resembling a villager, boarded the train with his wife and two children, ages eight and six. As the train traveled four or five li from Zhenru Station, the passenger suddenly collapsed and died. Passengers in the car were thrown into chaos. When the train attendant learned of this, he blew the whistle and immediately stopped the train, carrying the body off the train and placing it by the roadside. The passenger's wife pleaded with the attendant to take the body off the train at Zhenru Station, saying that the area was desolate and difficult to guard, but the attendant refused because of the hygiene of the passengers on the train. The wife was helpless and cried by the roadside, holding the body. The two children also cried with their mother. Fortunately, kind people in the area came forward to inquire. According to the passenger's wife, they lived in a village northwest of Nanxiang, more than ten li from the station. Her husband had no prior illnesses and was traveling to Shanghai with his children to attend a banquet at a relative's house and to have his frostbite on his feet treated. The villagers, seeing this, felt sorry for them and temporarily took in the two children and sent someone to accompany the wife to her home in Nanxiang. The family had no money to buy a coffin. The wife borrowed money from relatives to cover the body for three days and nights. Yesterday, the wife borrowed silver dollars to buy a coffin in Zhenru. She and her two children transported the coffin back, and before leaving, the wife and her two children prostrated themselves on the ground to thank the villagers.

Yixin Lane Tenant Appeals 118

▲ **Requesting Cancellation of Provisional Execution**

The Yixin Lane tenants and the owners, Cheng Linsheng and Cheng Yize, are involved in a lawsuit in the Special District Court over eviction issues. The court has ruled that the tenants should be evicted immediately and declared a provisional execution. The tenants have filed an appeal against the provisional execution, requesting an urgent disposition to advance the trial and cancel the declaration of provisional execution. The first reason is that the jurisdiction is wrong, stating that this case belongs to the local jurisdiction. Local Judge Yang Kai heard the case, and the summons also stated "Di Zi No. 452." Judge Yang did not express any objection to the jurisdiction, but suddenly changed it to a primary case. Therefore, they requested a correction regarding the declaration of disapproval of provisional execution, even if it belongs to a primary case, Article 464 of the Civil Procedure Law should also be applied ["If the debtor proves that the provisional execution may cause irreparable damage, the court should declare disapproval of the provisional execution according to the circumstances of Article 462 upon their request"]. And other various reasons. Yesterday morning, the civil court president Zhou Daren held a collegiate panel hearing. The tenants' lawyers Ye Fukang, Yu Hualong, and others were present, but Cheng Linsheng and others were not. Judge Ying then adjourned the hearing to another date.

January 12

Reader Communication

At Least Six Major Reforms Should Be Made in Politics 130

Speaking of political reform, one cannot help but sigh with exhaustion. The reform of Chinese politics has been going on for nearly thirty or forty years. In these decades, what has not been tried, such as constitutional monarchy, democratic republic, centralized power, one-party dictatorship? However, today's political phenomenon is still not on track, society is still in chaos, the economy is increasingly bankrupt, bandits are becoming more and more numerous, warlord separatism is still the same, and corruption is rampant. Recently, the Japanese have unreasonably occupied our entire Northeast. Let us look at Turkey after the Great War, which was oppressed by the Treaty of Mudros. All the coastal artillery positions of the straits were managed by the Allied forces, all warships had to be handed over, and all wireless, wired, and submarine cables were under the control of the Allied forces. Shipyards and all railways in the harbor were used by the Allied forces. Was not such a national situation even worse than China today? However, thanks to the leadership of Kemal, they were able to eliminate the corrupt old government internally and defeat the powerful Greek forces that manipulated them externally, and there was the Lausanne Conference that abolished unequal treaties. In less than ten years, Turkey has become a modern country again. In addition, the Japanese Restoration has been going on for less than sixty years, and the revival of Germany, which was defeated in the Great War, has only taken about ten years. Why has China not made any progress after thirty or forty years of reform? I believe that there are many and complex reasons for this, and the incomplete and insincere nature of political reform is also a major reason. In the future, if China's politics are to be on track, thorough and genuine reform, at least the existing politics should have the following six reforms: 1. Abolish the one-party dictatorship and implement party politics. One-party dictatorship is theoretically untenable and practically unworkable. Party politics is theoretically correct and has these advantages in practice: (A) Party politics is a natural political education, which can achieve the purpose of political tutelage. (B) Party politics is an effective political supervision, which can achieve progressive politics. (C) Party politics can gather national talents to jointly plan the great cause of the country. 2. Generate legitimate public opinion organs and promulgate a constitution representing public opinion. The constitution stipulates the rights and obligations of the people and the government, and the organs of public opinion are indispensable to any country. However, China did not have a provisional constitution until recently, and today there is still no legitimate organ representing public opinion. This is one of the reasons why politics is not on track. 3. The people's opinion and publication must be guaranteed by law and not subject to any illegal interference or oppression. Only in this way can strong and impartial public opinion be created. Only with impartial public opinion can there be right and wrong, and only with right and wrong can politics have a way. 4. Stop using national funds to fill party expenses. In theory, the party is part of the country and should not use public funds of the country as private expenses of a party. In fact, today's party departments in various places have lost the faith of the people, have no work, and cannot work. If they are not abolished, they will only be hated by the people. 5. In the current national crisis, we advocate imitating the national defense government organized by the French during the Franco-Prussian War, regardless of party affiliation, and the mixed cabinet recently organized by the British to deal with the economic crisis, to deal with the current Sino-Japanese problem. 6. In the current national crisis, we advocate that the Sino-Japanese problem should be decided by national referendum. The above six points, the first four points are the reforms that politics should have, and the latter two points are the reforms that should be made to deal with the current national crisis. I believe that it is the great way for China to rise from the dead. We citizens should rise up and strive for it. (Bing)

Education News

Important News 132

Normal School Students Must Serve Their Term Before Being Allowed to Further Their Education 133

▲Those Who Have Already Advanced Must Perform Service After Graduation

Several years ago, there were quite a few normal school graduates who went on to universities and colleges above the level of specialized schools. Later, the principals of provincial middle schools and the educational administrative authorities agreed that the public cultivation of normal school students was aimed at training elementary school teachers for local education. Even if normal school students wanted to pursue further studies and strive for advancement, they received free treatment from the public and were different from ordinary self-funded middle school graduates. Therefore, normal school graduates must undergo a considerable period of service after graduation to repay the public before they can advance to further studies. In the past two years, the educational administrative authorities have paid attention to implementing this matter. The Ministry of Education previously received a report from the Fujian Education Department, which was submitted by Xiamen University, a private university, asking whether this year's new students, who had graduated from senior high normal schools, should be allowed to make changes in their studies. The Ministry of Education instructed the department that senior high normal school graduates who have received free treatment must have proof of service before they are allowed to advance to further studies. Previously, the National Central University reported difficulties in handling this matter and requested instructions. It was instructed that since these students had been admitted, they should be allowed to retain their admission qualifications and enter the university in the next academic year after completing their service. For students who have no service opportunities, in order to take care of their studies, they are temporarily allowed to make special accommodations and wait until after graduation to complete their service to show compassion. However, this cannot be taken as an example in the future. The matter reported by Xiamen University is the same and should be handled in the same way.

Guangzhou Student Petition Group Arrives in Shanghai 136

▲The Petition's Purpose Consists of Nine Items

▲They Will Enter Beijing in a Day or Two

Guangzhou's entire student body, due to the recent loss of Jinzhou and the imminent danger to Pingjin, and the unified government's lack of concrete plans to save the country, organized a delegation of students from the entire city to petition in Beijing. The delegation will petition the government in Beijing. The delegation departed from Guangzhou on the eighth day and arrived in Shanghai yesterday (the twelfth). There are a total of 136 people. The purpose of the petition consists of nine items: (1) Request the government to immediately order the troops of various provinces to go to the Northeast to recover the lost territories. (2) Request the government to immediately dismiss and investigate Zhang Xueliang, who failed to defend the territory. (4) Request the government to execute Du Huang Qi within one week from the date of the petition. (5) Request the government not to directly negotiate with Japan until the Japanese army has withdrawn. (6) Request the government to dismiss and investigate the military police who shot and killed students (the leaders will be executed) and to allow the freedom of national salvation movements for the people in the future. (7) Request the government to urge Mr. Hu, Wang, and Jiang to immediately enter Beijing to preside over the great plan of saving the country. (8) Request the government to absolutely make public all finances in the future. (9) Request the government to report on the course of the loss of Jinzhou. If the government can satisfactorily answer the above nine demands and guarantee their earnest fulfillment, then the delegation will move south. The delegation is composed of three representatives from each school above the secondary level in Guangzhou, including Sun Yat-sen University, Lingnan University, Guangzhou University, National University, Guangzhou Law School, Provincial No. 1 Middle School, Provincial No. 2 Middle School, Provincial Women's Normal School, Provincial Vocational School, Municipal No. 1 Middle School, Municipal No. 2 Middle School, etc., consisting of more than fifty schools. They will rest in Shanghai for a day or two and then enter Beijing on a scheduled date.

The delegation of students from Nanjing University in the capital, urging Wang, Jiang, and Hu to come to Beijing, arrived in Shanghai at around 8:00 AM yesterday. The group consisted of more than four hundred and fifty people and sent representatives to visit Wang Jingwei and Feng Yuxiang at around 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon. The details are recorded as follows.

▲Delegation Officers: Head of the Delegation: Xu Ruixiang, Zhang Shude, Li Qitian, Li Rongguang, Zhang Zhaofu. Secretary-General: Zhao Zhangfu. Commander-in-Chief: Sun Yaohua. Deputy Commander: Pi Zonggan.

▲Representatives' Remarks: Zhang Shude, head of the delegation, said to the reporter of the China Society: "At a time when the country is in trouble, the central responsibility is borne by Mr. Wang, Jiang, and Hu, but the three gentlemen are not in Beijing, which has caused the government to lose its center of gravity and politics to fall into a state of despair. The students and others, based on their patriotism, do not hesitate to sacrifice their precious time to urge Mr. Wang, Jiang, and Hu to rush to Beijing to jointly face the national crisis. After staying in Shanghai for a short time to urge Wang, they will go to Fenghua to urge Jiang and Hong Kong to urge Hu. They will not return to Beijing until the goal is achieved."

▲Wang Was Sick and Did Not See Them: The delegation was afraid that there would be too many people and the actions would be inconvenient, so after arriving in Shanghai, they specially sent representatives Xu Ruixiang and Zhang Shude to Wang's residence on Pushi Road, hoping to meet Wang. However, Wang was sick in the hospital and could not see guests. The representatives handed the letter to Wang's residence for forwarding. The original letter is recorded as follows: "Mr. Jingwei, a great view. We, the entire student body of our school, are aware that the country is in a daily decline, foreign aggression is increasingly urgent, the central hub is vacant, and the center of gravity is falling. Therefore, regardless of everything, we have come to Shanghai to urge you to quickly go to Beijing and cooperate with Jiang and Hu to preside over the party and the country. Before this, we have sent Zhang Shude and Xu Ruixiang to visit and inquire about the time and place of the meeting. We respectfully present this and wish you a speedy recovery. Nanjing University Delegation Urging Wang, Jiang, and Hu to Go to Beijing."

▲Feng Expressed: At the same time, the delegation sent representatives Zhou Yintang, Li Qitian, Wang Wenbin, and Shen Naisen to visit Feng Yuxiang at Jiner West Road. Feng personally received them. After the representatives explained their intentions, Feng expressed his appreciation and talked for about ten minutes before leaving.

▲Reception of Reporters: The delegation is scheduled to hold a reception for the press at 10:00 AM today (the 13th) in the Student Union Office of the Upper Institute of Jiaotong University. Due to the hasty time, no further notice was given.

The Western Green Basketball Team Wins Three Consecutive Championships 145

▲ John Had the Will but Not the Strength

▲ Failed 50 to 21 Yesterday

￣↓Tonight, Group B Finals↓

The John University basketball team fell short. In yesterday's final against the Pirates, they still lost 50 to 21. Thus, the Pirates won the Western Green Basketball Championship for the third year in a row. The Pirates were unstoppable, exerting relentless pressure on John from beginning to end, leaving them overwhelmed. The Pirates' long shots were particularly wonderful, beyond description and irresistible. In the first half, the score was 21 to 6. The referees were Zhang Guodong and inspector Xu Zhendong. There was also a Group A game, which Qingguang won. The first half score was 17 to 12, resulting in a final score of 32 to 27.

Reasons for John's Failure 146

Less than three minutes into the game, John lost six points in a row due to inadequate defense. Haines shot from the corner of the basket, Lin Zequn headed it in himself, and Euler shot from long range. Mysteriously, they lost three goals in a row. First, their luck with the ball was poor, and they could not penetrate under the basket, with most attempts failing due to inaccurate rebound angles. Second, the Pirates were accurate with long-range shots under the basket, hitting the mark every time with incredible skill. Third, while the Pirates' shooting guards were skilled, John's defense was lax, with gaps appearing frequently. In the first half, they used a five-man zone defense, but the Pirates crisscrossed and shot from long range with ease. Although they switched to a man-to-man defense in the second half, their running and turning were not as quick as the Pirates. Given these three shortcomings, how could John not lose? If the Pirates continue to dominate, where will valiant athletes rise up to defeat them? It is a pity that the Northeast University basketball team has become a historical term today; otherwise, they would surely give the Pirates a head-on blow.

Free Talk

Talking About the Fall of Jinzhou to the Japanese 150

— Zheng Yimei

The Japanese bandits' iron cavalry advanced rapidly and directly, and Jinzhou has fallen. The place is twenty-five li from the Nuer River. It was established as a state in Liaoning and a prefecture in the Qing Dynasty, belonging to Shengjing. It was abolished in the Republic of China. Today's Jin County is its old governance. At the end of the Ming Dynasty, Zu Dashou defended Jinzhou. Upon hearing of the loss of Songshan, he surrendered the city to the Qing Dynasty. This place has been contested by military strategists, not just starting today. To the west is the Xiaoling River, to the north is the Shajia Cemetery, and Tangjiatun is to the east. There are sedans and large carts for transportation, where sedans carry people, and large carts transport goods, which is very convenient. Markets are all in the city, and there are very few markets outside the city. In the city is the Great Buddha Temple, which has a pagoda thirty zhang high, said to have been built in the Tang Dynasty. The people are mostly superstitious in divine power. Every year on the eighteenth day of the abolished lunar April, there is a Niangniang Fair. There are also the Dizang Fair on April 28th and the City God Fair on May 28th. There are various operas and other performances to please the gods and pray for blessings, with people exerting all their efforts for them. Nearby are Guanyin Cave and Jinniu Cave. From late summer to early autumn, the vegetation is lush, and men and women come to visit in an endless stream, especially painters sketching from life, as the scenery is beautiful and the location is excellent for painting. Products include shrimp oil pickles, felt strips, felt hats and shoes, pigs, pig bristles, wool, beans, and bean cakes, all transported to Tianjin, Yingkou, and other places for sale, and business is thriving. This time, the Japanese people have been rampant, and the loss is greater than ever before. The Japanese people take burning and killing as a display of power and rape as pleasure. A certain soldier once broke into the Wang family in Xiaoxinmintun. The young widow of the Wang family was quite beautiful. The soldier wanted to defile her. The woman deliberately kept him to drink. When he was drunk, the woman struck the soldier's head with a wine jar. She hit with great force, breaking his head and causing brain matter to flow out, killing him. Knowing that she had caused trouble, the woman immediately took poison and committed suicide. Those who heard about it said that since the Republic of China, the world has been declining, and there have been very few reports of women's chastity and martyrdom. Anyone who talks about it is branded as pedantic. Unexpectedly, in the midst of national crisis, there is such a moving and praiseworthy story, which is truly rare. A guest returning from Beiping mentioned it, so I specifically praise it. It is also the responsibility of us writers.

Cheng Yanqiu Takes Students in the South 151

— Si Ren

On New Year's Day, Xun Huisheng had his eldest son, Lingxiang, study with Cheng Yuqiu. A banquet was held at Fengzeyuan to perform the apprenticeship ceremony. At 5 PM that afternoon, Huisheng led Lingxiang to Cheng's residence to respectfully welcome Yuqiu to Fengzeyuan. Many guests brought congratulatory couplets. Here are some of the best ones. Huilu's couplet said, "Cheng's gate stands in the snow," "Xun's son is like a dragon." Liu Xiaosang's couplet said, "Jade is moist and frost is clear, reflecting the three-foot snow of Cheng's gate," "The inkstone pond is autumn water, adding a few fragrances to Xun's order." And also, "Snow tablets serve Yichuan, and good young masters are seen in this turbid world," "Bamboo books carry dark solutions, and old friends enjoy having virtuous fathers and brothers." At six o'clock, the apprenticeship ceremony was held. After the ceremony, they entered the banquet. The guests pushed Liu Xiaosang to deliver a congratulatory speech, which briefly said, "Today is the New Year's Day holiday. Yuqiu will soon go abroad to study theatrical arts, making his first grand tour. Lingxiang also takes Yuqiu as his teacher today, which is truly an unprecedented grand event. I hope Lingxiang will not only learn Yuqiu's popular tunes, but also continue Yuqiu's great cause of reforming drama, then his achievements should be above those of ordinary famous actors." Then Xu Lingxiao gave a speech, which briefly said, "Yuqiu's becoming a school is not only due to his tunes. His thoughts and talents are increasingly moving towards the mission of drama, which is beyond the reach of ordinary people. And he will soon go to Europe to study, which will greatly enhance the art of drama. It is truly an unprecedented feat in the drama world. Now Lingxiang is seeking knowledge at this time, which is of great significance. I hope Yuqiu will teach him carefully so that Lingxiang can become someone who has contributed to the art of drama. Therefore, I use two lines of opera lyrics, 'The father is a hero, the son is a good man, and there are no weak soldiers under a strong general' to congratulate Lingxiang." At this point, the guests asked Yuqiu to give a reply. Yuqiu briefly said, "Today is the first day of my thirtieth year. It is also the first day that I changed my name to Yanqiu. It is also the first day that I have enrolled disciples. Confucius said that at thirty, one should be established. This establishment means being able to stand up. This standing up is not easy. I am thirty years old, so I changed the word 'Yan' in 'Yanli' to the word 'Yan' in 'Yantian.' My inkstone field is still reclaiming barren land. However, farmers who plant fields hope to harvest. Confucius also said, 'The problem with people is that they like to be teachers.' I cannot stand up yet. How can I suddenly become a teacher, isn't it a contradiction? But I accept Lingxiang as a disciple for two reasons. First, because Lingxiang is smart and studies English and arithmetic, and he is quite diligent. That's why I'm willing to be his teacher. Second, because Huisheng is my senior. His art is brilliant. If I don't teach well, he will correct it. So I dare to be his teacher. The gateway to learning drama must first learn Kunqu to lay the foundation. Mr. Wang Bosheng said that he must first learn spoken drama. I highly agree because spoken drama has no music to rely on. Its inner performance is especially difficult. I hope Lingxiang will work hard on it." Then Huisheng gave a reply, which briefly said, "Yuqiu's words are too polite. My art is not brilliant. I can't teach my son, so I ordered my son to seek teaching from someone brilliant. What the gentlemen said is to maintain art, and I have benefited a lot. I am especially grateful for your love for my little son. Please everyone drink a big white one." After leaving the seats, a group photo was taken, and the guests and hosts parted happily.

World Anecdotes 152

— Hai Ke

The True Value of the Human Body: Human beings have different statuses, whether rich or poor, noble or lowly, intelligent or foolish, virtuous or unworthy. Therefore, there is a distinction between ordinary people and important figures. If you were to assess the true value of their bodies, then regardless of wealth or poverty, nobility or lowliness, intelligence or foolishness, virtue or unworthiness, they are all exactly the same. British biologist Dr. I. ErLaW. son recently gave a speech somewhere, giving a chemical analysis of the human body. According to him, taking an ordinary human body weighing one hundred and forty pounds as an example, it can be known that the water contained in this body can fill a ten-gallon bucket. All the fat can make seven bars of soap. All the carbon can make nine hundred pencils. All the phosphorus can make two thousand two hundred match heads. All the magnesium can make a dose of salt. All the iron can make a medium-sized nail. All the lime can whitewash a chicken coop. All the sulfur can kill fleas on a dog. Counting the true value of these materials, calculated at current market prices, you only need five shillings to buy them. Therefore, it is not unreasonable to say that each human body is only worth five shillings.

Going on an Expedition 153

— A Member of the Youth Supporting Horse Troop

(10) Summary of the Beijing-Shanghai Section (Continued)

Our life is very simple because we are a national salvation team. Everything is militarized. Before dawn, a bugle sounds, and hundreds of warriors gather in the open space to practice. When the sun is in the middle of the sky, the bugle sounds again, and we each take a mouthwash utensil to fill with food and satiate our hunger. When the sun sets in the west, the bugle sounds again, and we eat in the same way as before. When the moon rises in the east, the bugle sounds again, and we quickly spread our bedding on the ground, and two or three people cover themselves with a cotton batting and go to rest. If the bugle sounds suddenly, then you can't care whether you are dreaming of being a rich man or having a wonderful dream of a wedding night. You rub your eyes and brave the cold to receive orders.

Our comrades are very loyal. "Everyone eats together when there is food, and everyone does things when there is work." Truly, that's what we all think. But when eating, we are honestly not polite because we are afraid that "politeness" will become a habit. If we are also polite when killing the enemy in the front, wouldn't that be terrible?

We slept in the car for two nights in Nanjing. The form of sleeping was very unique. The first person lay on the shoulder of the second person, and the second person also lay on the shoulder of the third person. It was quite comfortable to lie down like this one by one. However, one comrade had a body as short as a Japanese pirate, so his head could only lean on the arm of the next person. Another comrade had a torso that was particularly thin and long, so his head could press on the neck of the next person. From the moment when the snoring shook the mountains and rivers, I peered around and saw these long and short heads, and couldn't help but laugh.

Sometimes, before going to sleep, we hold a foot-washing conference.

A Letter About the Recent Art Scene in Paris (Part 1) 154

— Liu Kang

This is a recent letter that comrade Liu Kang sent me from France, describing the situation of the current Autumn Salon in Paris and the lives of artists, which is even more detailed than my previous "European Correspondence." I think there must be many readers who want to hear about the latest news from the Paris art scene, so I asked the editor of this publication to publish this letter. I will briefly declare it as a small introduction. I don't think Liu Kang will blame me for being nosy? January 1, 1932, Hai Li, Shanghai Cuntian Pavilion.

Teacher Hai... I don't know how many times I've started writing, wanting to make a detailed report on the Autumn Exhibition; but... lazy? Busy? I also inexplicably ended up procrastinating without results. This is really unfortunate. This morning, I received a letter from November 9th, reading it made people excited, so I had to start writing again, I think this time I shouldn't fail again!

The Autumn Exhibition opened on October 1st (until December 13th). Generally speaking, it is much the same as last year. The center of attention of the entire venue is again focused on Bonnard's two new works... a landscape of delicate tones and a golden-colored portrait of a girl... one is quiet and mysterious, the other is passionate and active. In short, the means of operating color can be said to have reached the extreme. Asselin has improved a lot compared to last year. Two size 40 portraits of adults and children were appropriately hung next to Bonnard's two, which is very interesting! Because comparing them with each other, one shows the richness of his color, and the other further confirms the solidity of his texture. Kisling's painting this time can be regarded as the crystallization of his lifelong flower paintings, with a very deep interest in porcelain. The female painter Marval's "Dream" writes the fantasy of a young woman's desire for wealth and honor, which is extremely vivid, with gorgeous colors and majestic brushstrokes. Sonverbie's Hellenized figures are both lovely and respectable. Blanc made a very large-scale picture, entitled Before the Wedding; excitement and joy are fully expressed. As for Van Dongen, I feel very sorry for him. The two portraits of celebrities (political celebrity Riberton and Paibleve) do have some unfaithfulness (faithful to art) and insincerity (sincere to people, sincere to oneself) that are below mediocrity. Tempted by profit and fame, the artist's personality is swept away! In addition, Laprade, Espagnat, etc. neither advance nor retreat, just like in previous years, and there is no need to repeat them.

I borrowed a large vat from someone in advance and filled it with clean warm water. Then groups of comrades stretched their legs into the vat to swim. The female comrades were also like this. It was very interesting.

Finally, there are still two-thirds of the journey to the Northeast. We still need to stay in Nanjing for a few days before advancing as a whole division. Compatriots, I wish you all the best for the country. I will report more news from the future later.

Exhibition Notes of the China Art College 155

— Wei Qi

The national painting style of the China Art College is the purest and most natural in Shanghai. The painting path is unique and upright. Generally, landscapes look up to the Yuan masters from Wen Tang, while flower and bird paintings adhere to the boneless method of hooking in the Northern and Southern Song Dynasties and are imbued with the spirit of Baiyang Xinluo. This is due to the good teaching of masters such as Xin Hu, Shizi Gongzhan, Hongwei Mengrong, Wuchang Manqing, and Jiekang, as well as the good learning of the students, so they were successful. Qi Weixin regards the Art College as his alma mater and is now in charge of teaching in the school. The rules still follow Ma Zheng. It can be said that Xihe is to Zhusi. This time, the school's fourth graduation exhibition is full of masterpieces. Graduates such as Huang Jinghua, Fang Jiangshui, Dai Tinghe, and Zuo Dequan are all excellent choices. Among the students at the school, there are Xu Hui's landscapes, Qu Zongxie's animals, and Lu Xiaying, Liu Shen, Xie Jun, Huang Dacong, and Ding Bao's flower and bird paintings. All of them have brushwork and charm. The autumn harvest has not yet arrived, but the spring flowers are worth appreciating. Lu Cha is a strange sight. The world is in great turmoil. Ms. He Xiangning is advocating saving the country with calligraphy and painting, then the achievements of the Art College's colleagues in art, the contribution to society, and saving and loving the country can all be divined at this meeting.

The Record of Rong Shuanglou (8) 157

— Seeking Happiness, the Master of Qi

Chapter 1: A Famous Courtesan Secluded, Misses Her Beautiful Partner, A Student Wandering in a Foreign Land, Builds a Strange Romance

It's just that his temperament is a little frivolous, and he has always lived a life of abundance. With his family constantly supplying his expenses, he inevitably likes to compete with a group of useless friends in recreational and playing fields during his spare time and holidays. Relying on his extraordinary appearance, handsome clothes, generous actions, and refined temperament, he has gatherings with playboys and the flattery of beautiful women everywhere. He almost acts like a playboy. Through a friend who is an English teacher in the Liang family, he got to know this romantic and suave Liang Xiaoyun. Counting the time, they have been friends for seven or eight months, and they can be considered unusually compatible with each other.

He admires her famous beauty, and she admires his handsome luxury. Whenever there are good mornings and evenings, he often comes to her house to open his heart and chat intimately. Occasionally, they also walk hand in hand together, traveling in famous gardens and scenic spots, dancing and singing. At first glance, they look like a beautiful couple. In her heart, this has been through numerous thorough investigations and careful considerations. She deeply feels that An Yutian is like a piece of uncarved jade. Coupled with his masculine demeanor, athletic body, scholarly articles, and chivalrous style, they all meet her ideal lover's conditions. It's just a pity that he is a bit stubborn by nature, and his circumstances are not poor. It seems he cannot lower his head and heart to rely on her pomegranate skirt and obediently obey her command training, acting like a love-captive gentleman. If he only seeks harmony and is merely a temporary union of wild mandarin ducks between the Sang and Jian rivers, or compromises and humbly retreats to a side room like the story of Lian Qing, who pities her fate, then all of this is beyond her original wishes and cannot be accommodated in this way. Moreover, it would needlessly change her original intention and lose the entire game, which is no different from lightly cutting off this opportunity and turning it into a mistake that is too hasty. How can she know that if she persists, there may not be a gap to take advantage of? Therefore, she is cautious and expectant, hesitant and hesitant, and has never revealed any trace of what to look for. And An Yutian is broad-minded and careless. Although he feels that this exquisite and transparent beauty is a rare beauty, often between intentional and unintentional, their hearts are in sync, and their eyes are provocative, which is indeed not bad for him. However, looking closely at her noble and invincible demeanor, she seems to have a demeanor worthy of an immortal.

Silver Dollar Market Unusually Slack 161

▲ Market Overview The financial industry in the 20th year was affected by various major impacts, especially the occurrence of many unfortunate difficulties in commerce, resulting in economic conditions that could not be remedied. Financial adjustments were very difficult. Although the transition through the year-end was said to be smooth, the majority of difficult hurdles lie in the abolition of the traditional Chinese New Year (i.e., mid-early February in the Gregorian calendar). Therefore, the current distance is not far, and financial constraints are precisely due to this major malady. It is appropriate that the current market is bleak and the public is idle, a situation even more pronounced than in previous years. Yesterday, the unremarkable tranquility of the interest rate on the money market was almost entirely due to this.

Because the current benchmark market value is actually very cheap, distributors from foreign ports can all calculate it, so although the year-end is near, the sales are more vigorous. The near and far terms saw a boost due to good actual sales. The trend of May and June, when factory dumping was very quiet, was also good. As a result, this month rose by 7 li and a half from the previous day, February rose by 1 fen and a half, March and April rose by 1 fen and 2 li and a half, May rose by 2 fen and 6 li, and June rose by 2 fen and a half, it is said.

Wheat Factory Needs Can be Expected to Increase 169

▲ Distant-term Short Positions are Heavily Covered

Yesterday, the market in day-term wheat showed an initial stabilization and continued to rise. Due to the delivery relationship in the current month, there were very few entries and exits. Distant-term short positions were covered, and because the flour market turned up, public sentiment also improved. According to the current situation, if foreign wheat does not create a setback, the needs of the factory can be expected to increase. If so, the foundation of the wheat market may turn stable. However, the button for rising and falling still depends on whether foreign wheat can come to a peak. As a result, the current month rose by 2 fen and 2 from the previous day, February rose by 6 fen, March rose by 5 fen, April and May rose by 6 fen, and June rose by 5 fen, it is said.

North-South Goods, Golden Needles, Vegetable Fungus All See Opportunities 170

▲ Golden Needles Recently, the sales of Guangdong, Hong Kong, and Shantou groups have become more active, and the market situation has rebounded. The number of transactions for several consecutive days has been quite considerable. The sales in Guangdong and Hong Kong have been sluggish for a long time. Now that the market price has reached a low level, they have started to stock up in preparation for spring sales. The selling price has risen by more than 2 taels from before. Yesterday, the selling price of top-quality vegetables in the city was around 23 taels, and gradually from 21 taels to 17-18 taels, with the trend gradually entering a stable path.

▲ Fungus The asking price for Sichuan goods is no less than 70 taels. The current market has risen to 72 taels. It is even more difficult to negotiate the price in the Han market, with a difference of 10 taels. The sales here have suddenly increased recently, and the selling price has rebounded by 4-5 taels for several consecutive days. Ordinary miscellaneous fungus sells for 70 taels, and higher-quality goods are priced higher. Guangdong groups have also taken action because the price has rebounded, so there is hope for the future, it is said.

Silk, Tea, White Raw, Difficult to Rise Despite US Telegram 171

Yesterday, the foreign silk market in this port was still difficult to activate. Although there was a telegram from New York regarding the silk from Bai Li, the New York Raw Silk Exchange only opened the recent silk at 1.61 US dollars per pound and the distant-term silk at 1.70 US dollars. The price was still difficult to rise. Yesterday, Bai Li bought 10 packages of Huang Raw, and Shen Yu and others bought 15 packages of Gan Da Raw. The price was still flat and weak.

Spring Dry Cocoon Goods Lack, Asking Price Steadily Firm 172

▲ Silk Ben Still Needs to Pull 850-860 Taels Per Hundred Catties

Last year, the spring raw in various counties in Jiangsu and Zhejiang suffered from improper weather conditions. The cocoon production was great, the cocoon quality was less than ideal, and there were more inferior products. According to statistics, the spring cocoons produced in Jiangsu and Zhejiang were not enough for the various silk factories to produce. Fortunately, the sales in Europe and the United States plummeted, and there was still some surplus of spring cocoons, and the bottom had the price of cocoons. The current market price of ordinary spring dry cocoons is 520-30 catties, which converts to a cocoon price of 163-4 taels per dan. Silk ben still needs to pull 850-60 taels per hundred catties.

Wuyuan Zhenmei European Sales Continue to be Smooth 173

Yesterday, Wuyuan Beigao Road Zhuang Zhenmei green tea feared that Hechang line and other firms were still buying, never loosening. The total number of transactions citywide was over 200 crates. The top tier cocoon was sold at 144 taels, no great difference from the previous day. The city still has over 2000 crates of unsold high-tier Zhuang Zhenmei. Heard that British brokers have already sent telegrams, canvassing for old goods. Though they are not to be taken lightly.

Small Forum

Important People Busying Themselves on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway · Fortunately 177

│Who are they busying themselves for, rushing back and forth?

The Beijing-Shanghai Railway seems to have been specially built for important people. Going to Beijing and leaving Beijing, rushing back and forth. If someone were to record the important people coming and going on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway every day of the year, they could compile a very thick record of the comings and goings of dignitaries on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway every year.

To prove my point, I randomly picked up this newspaper from New Year's Day onwards and checked the itineraries of the people of the time recorded each day. The result of the inspection... was that on December 31st of the twentieth year, Zhu Peide, Zhu Lixue, and Yang Hu left Beijing and arrived in Shanghai at 5:00 PM that afternoon. That evening, Yu Youren, Chen Shaokuan, and Kong Xiangxi went to Beijing. There were no reports for the five days after New Year's Day, so the itineraries of important people during these five days cannot be checked. Chen Mingshu arrived in Shanghai on the evening of the 7th; Zhang Jingjiang, Liu Luyin, and Liu Ruiheng arrived in Shanghai on the morning of the 8th. That evening, Chen Shaokuan, Zhu Jiahua, Tang Shengzhi, and Ye Kaixin went to Beijing; Sun Ke, Huang Liang, and Yu Youren arrived in Shanghai on the 9th. That evening, Chen Mingshu went to Beijing; He Yingqin and Chen Youren arrived in Shanghai on the 10th. That evening, Chen returned to Beijing; Chu Minyi left Beijing on the evening of the 11th. That evening, Liu Ruiheng went to Beijing. Chu arrived in Shanghai on the morning of the 12th. From December 31st of last year to today, excluding five days, which is only a week, the records of important people coming to Shanghai and going to Beijing are quite impressive.

Officials have official duties, and those who are officials should abide by their [duties] and uphold their [responsibilities]. They should not lightly leave their posts unless absolutely necessary, especially in these times of national crisis. Those who are officials should diligently attend to their duties, so much so that they fear that not even working day and night is enough to alleviate the national crisis and meet the people's expectations. We dare to ask this group of important people going to Beijing and leaving Beijing, rushing back and forth on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, what exactly are they doing?

Nanjing is the political center, and major plans concerning the national economy and the people's livelihood should be handled in Nanjing. Apart from the new Minister of Finance, Huang Hanliang, who has to come to Shanghai to discuss raising funds and liaise with the financial community, what exactly are the rest coming to Shanghai for? For the national economy and the people's livelihood? But Shanghai is not a political center!

If it is not for the national economy and the people's livelihood, not for official business, then it must be for private affairs. They eat the food of the common people and take the money of the common people. When the country is in crisis and the people are suffering, they leisurely travel to Shanghai for private affairs, ignoring politics and neglecting their duties. They come and go on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, requiring specially prepared free railway cars and specially dispatched soldiers to greet and send them off. In addition to the individual, they sometimes bring their wives, young masters, young ladies, and a large group of attendants and orderlies. This is not only dereliction of duty, not only failing the country and the people, but also harming the country and the people. What do we the people need such officials for?

When Mr. Hu Hanmin was the Speaker of the Legislative Yuan, he never left Beijing and never came to Shanghai. This is a point worth praising. An [official] who bears heavy political responsibilities often comes to this Shanghai of gilded palaces and dissipated pleasures. Whether he still has the leisure to consider the national economy and the people's livelihood is self-evident! What exactly are you, a group of people rushing back and forth on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, doing?

Two New Year Songs That Should Not Be Forgotten · Ze · Pu 178

My teacher, Mr. Qi Fu, who does not remove the weeds in his courtyard, wrote three New Year songs in the 17th year of the Republic of China, which are quite sufficient to warn the world. Ze accidentally found them in the teacher's diary. Although they are already outdated, in the face of the current national crisis, I would like to introduce two of them as follows, hoping to encourage all readers:

㈠Written for Young Students

Listen! The rooster has already crowed.

Look! The candlelight is dim.

The plan for the year begins on January 1st.

Classmates, rise!

Comrades, rise!

Quickly get up and bow - willing to offer the intellect

Together with the body,

To the Republic of China, vowing to start from this year, this day!

㈡Written for National Salvation Warriors

Listen! The rooster has already crowed.

Look! The candlelight is dim.

Four hundred million people are buried alive in hell.

Compatriots, rise!

Compatriots, rise!

Quickly get up and go to the front!

A rifle,

A horse;

Seize the heads of national traitors,

To dye this New Year, this new day!

Popular Science

Air Pressure Crushes a Tin Can · Zhou · Rui · Quan 179

Scrape! Yi Xin heard this loud sound and ran into the room in a panic, seeing a crushed small tin can in a basin on the table. His brother, Huan Xin, stood beside him grinning, looking very happy.

Yi Xin│Brother! What was that sound just now?

Huan Xin│[I'm doing an interesting experiment.

Look, isn't there a crushed tin can in the middle of this basin of water? This tin can was originally a good one. Just now, with a scrape, it was the sound it made when it acted up.]

Yi Xin│[How did it make that sound, and how did it get crushed?]

Huan Xin│[I took a good can, opened a small round hole in the middle of the top of the can, took out the vegetables, poured in a quarter of water, lit a fire to boil it, and then tightly sealed the hole with a wooden stopper (if it's not tight, or apply fire lacquer or other things that can seal the hole).

) Put it in the basin of water. After only five or six minutes, it scraped, and the tin can suddenly collapsed.]

Yi Xin│[What's the reason for this?]

Huan Xin│[Because there was only a quarter of water in the tin can. After being boiled by the fire, the steam completely expelled the air in the can. The top was sealed, with only full of steam inside. When it was thrown into the basin of cold water, after about five or six minutes, the steam cooled down and completely turned into cold water. The tin can became a vacuum. We know that the atmospheric pressure is very high, about fifteen pounds of pressure per square inch. The can cooled down, and there was nothing inside except a little water, so it was subjected to atmospheric pressure and collapsed with a scrape. The reason why the can collapsed was originally because of the pressure of the large amount of air outside. Isn't this an interesting thing?]

East, West, South, North

Banking King Morgan 180

This banking king, Z. B. Morgan, started by selling the art collection that his father loved and obtaining a lot of cash. At that time, everyone in his family opposed it in unison, and people gave him selfish and stingy bad reviews. However, the stubborn and confident Z. B. ignored the opposition of his family and the criticism of the world, and silently carried out his confidence. Then, was he really stingy? In fact, it was definitely not like that.

In fact, all that his father left him were these art collections and property equal to the debts he owed, such as worthless stocks and 19 million in cash. However, he had to pay 3 million in inheritance tax, had to distribute the property according to the will, and had to operate a huge business. Therefore, he was indeed in the difficult situation of having to sell the art collection that his father loved. He resolutely carried it out, and then he saved the family fortune and succeeded as the great banking king Morgan. Therefore, he not only became the ruler of the American financial world, but also lent 1.5 billion yuan to the Allied countries during the war, absorbed millions of gold blocks from Europe, and saved the European countries from the brink of life and death with millions of yuan of weapons and food. Sure enough, he became an even greater banking king than his father.

Copper King Guggenheim 181

[My copper mine is about to go bankrupt now, can you help me?] Guggenheim's friend asked him.

[Oh! That's pitiful!]

Guggenheim, who was rich in friendship and chivalry, took out money to save his friend's copper mine. This was the beginning of his copper kingdom.

After he decided to help his friend run the copper mine, he carefully planned it in his mind, and then he called his sons to talk.

[We don't know when the business we are doing now will develop. Let's join forces to engage in copper mining.]

The sons all agreed very much, so his copper mining business started from then on. Especially his third son, Daniel, was even more daring. Soon, a large copper mining kingdom with an annual output of 500,000 tons, accounting for one-half of the world's industry, was built in this way.

If anyone asked Daniel Guggenheim's secret to success, he would immediately answer:

[Sacrifice! Sacrifice! Sacrifice!]

Shanghai Stories

Shanghai Stories (7) Compiled and Translated by Zhou Rong 182

×The Earliest Trade and Tariffs

After the opening of the trading port, the Su Song Tai Dao designated six money shops to issue receipts for import and export taxes and tonnage dues. British Consul Balfour protested, believing that it violated the treaty, for fear that British business would be monopolized by a few people. The British Consul originally wanted to stipulate that tariffs would not be paid before foreign goods arrived at the port and were sold, but this was rejected by the Imperial Commissioner.

Within the first six weeks after the opening of the port, that is, from November 14th to December 31st, only seven merchant ships entered the port. The total value of imported goods was 433,729 taels, and the total value of exported goods was 147,172 taels. The import tax collected was 16,564 taels and 8 mace; the export tax was 7,537 taels, 1 mace, and 9 fen. A total of 985 taels of tonnage dues were collected, which was much lower than the tonnage dues previously collected in Guangzhou.

×The Beginning of Extraterritoriality

The so-called extraterritoriality means that foreigners in Chinese territory are not subject to Chinese law but are subject to the jurisdiction of their country's consuls stationed in China, so it is also called consular jurisdiction.

The Treaty of Nanjing did not explicitly recognize that foreigners enjoyed extraterritoriality in Chinese trading ports, but Articles 15, 16, and 17 of the Sino-British Supplementary Treaty in May of the eighth year of Xianfeng, as well as Articles 22 and 28 of the Sino-American Treaty in May of the same year, explicitly recognized that foreigners enjoyed extraterritoriality in Chinese trading ports.

Article 17 of the Sino-British Supplementary Treaty in the eighth year of Xianfeng stated; [In the event that British nationals accuse Chinese nationals, they should first go to the consular office to file a complaint. The consul should immediately investigate the cause and first try to resolve the matter peacefully to avoid litigation. If Chinese people go to the consul to accuse British nationals, the consul should also try to resolve the matter peacefully. If the matter cannot be resolved peacefully, the Chinese local officials and the consul shall jointly try the case fairly.]

Article 27 of the Sino-American Treaty says··[If citizens of the United States have disputes over property in Chinese trading ports, they shall be investigated and handled by their consuls and other officials. If citizens of the United States have disputes with people trading in China from other countries, both parties should be heard and handled in accordance with the treaties established by their respective countries. Chinese officials shall not interfere.]

Article 28 also says··

[If citizens of the United States have important matters to litigate with Chinese local officials, they should first report to the consuls and other officials. After confirming that the wording in the report is clear and the matter is reasonable, they will forward it to the local officials for investigation. Chinese merchants are allowed to submit reports to the local officials on the one hand and to the consuls and other officials on the other hand for investigation. If Chinese people and citizens of the United States have disputes that cannot be resolved peacefully, the officials of the two countries must investigate, discuss, and decide on the matter fairly. No fees may be charged, and people may be invited to the court to act as interpreters to avoid misunderstandings due to language barriers]

Since the signing of these treaties, foreigners have been able to enjoy extraterritoriality in Chinese territory and are not subject to Chinese law. Therefore, bandits run rampant within the concessions, committing all kinds of evil. Shanghai has become a den of sin in the Far East, all due to these unequal treaties.

Regulations for Soliciting Articles for the Local Supplementary Publication 184

㈠ Various essays on literary and social topics, such as (1) poems and short essays related to current affairs (2) essays that improve, criticize, or satirize society

㈠ In addition to the above two types, this publication also welcomes other extremely interesting and valuable essays. However, please note that all articles should preferably be related to Shanghai facts.

㈠ Articles should be concise and preferably around 400-500 words, and should not exceed 800 words at most.

㈠ Manuscripts should be written vertically and the characters should not be sloppy. Western paper should not be used, and Western text should be omitted where possible.

㈠ A seal must be affixed to the manuscript for verification when collecting remuneration in the future. ㈠ Please indicate that the envelope for submissions should be addressed to the Editorial Department of the Local Supplementary Publication ㈠ All submissions will not be returned regardless of whether they are published. If a return is required, it should be stated in advance and a postage stamp of one cent or four cents should be attached.

㈠ Remuneration for articles is divided into three grades: A, B, and C. Grade A is four yuan, Grade B is three yuan, and Grade C is two yuan. Special articles will be remunerated separately.
